  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_fc7046b5-a7d8-4a52-908a-29b8d3116328'

<span id="freeTextContainer11544501418224482601">To Whom it May Concern, <br/><br/>It was easy to call us forbidden and harder to call us soulmates. Yet I believed we were both.   <span id="freeText11544501418224482601" style="display:none">To Whom it May Concern, <br /><br />It was easy to call us forbidden and harder to call us soulmates. Yet I believed we were both. Forbidden soulmates. <br /><br />When I arrived to Edgewood, Wisconsin I didn’t plan to find him. I didn't plan to stumble into Joe's bar and have Daniel's music stir up my emotions. I had no clue that his voice would make my hurts forget their own sorrow. I had no idea that my happiness would remember its own bliss. <br /><br />When I started senior year at my new school, I wasn’t prepared to call him Mr. Daniels, but sometimes life happens at the wrong time for all the right reasons. <br /><br />Our love story wasn’t only about the physical connection.<br /><br />It was about family. It was about loss. It was about being alive. It was silly. It was painful. It was mourning. It was laughter.<br /><br />It was ours. <br /><br />And for those reasons alone, I would never apologize for <i>Loving Mr. Daniels</i>. <br /><br />-Ashlyn Jennings</span>

<a href="/questions/1139881-i-really-loved-this-book-specifically">I really loved this book. Specifically, the teacher/student aspect. Can anyone suggest very similar titles to this one? The characters were so relatable and believable. That&#39;s the part that got me most. Thanks!</a>
</div>

<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/55607584-shavonda"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1462551327i/55607584._UX100_CR0,33,100,100_.jpg" /></a>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Slammed by Colleen Hoover; To Professor with Love by Linda Kage; On the Island by Tracey Garvis Graves; Waking Olivia by Elizabeth O'Roark. All four o<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Slammed by Colleen Hoover; To Professor with Love by Linda Kage; On the Island by Tracey Garvis Graves; Waking Olivia by Elizabeth O'Roark. All four of these have a teacher/student "forbidden" storyline but nothing grotesque and no underage sexual relationships. <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/930464665?book_show_action=true">May 07, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Christy by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/6744426-anna">Anna</a>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer930464665" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14558057102783227303"><b>Maximum amount of stars I can give ♥</b> <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/e59c906b-f4ea-4cba-9bf0-2109209f5864_zps5e0f36d2.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1401425822i/9801333.jpg' alt=' photo e59c906b-f4ea-4cba-9bf0-2109209f5864_zps5e0f36d2.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I think that it is very possible that I just found my favorite book of 2014. <i>Loving Mr. Daniel’s</i> was THAT GOOD. I can’t think of one thing I didn’t love about this story. The impact it had on me was major. I laughed, I cried, I loved every single page. I can’t recommend this one enough. <br/><br/>Ashlyn Jennings is a girl after my own heart...<br/><i>
  <blockquote> You know what the best thing about purses was? They could carry around books.</blockquote>
</i> But on a more serious note, Ashlyn has de</span>
  <span id="freeText14558057102783227303" style="display:none"><b>Maximum amount of stars I can give ♥</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/e59c906b-f4ea-4cba-9bf0-2109209f5864_zps5e0f36d2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1401425822i/9801333.jpg" alt=" photo e59c906b-f4ea-4cba-9bf0-2109209f5864_zps5e0f36d2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I think that it is very possible that I just found my favorite book of 2014. <i>Loving Mr. Daniel’s</i> was THAT GOOD. I can’t think of one thing I didn’t love about this story. The impact it had on me was major. I laughed, I cried, I loved every single page. I can’t recommend this one enough. <br><br>Ashlyn Jennings is a girl after my own heart...<br><i>
  <blockquote> You know what the best thing about purses was? They could carry around books.</blockquote>
</i> But on a more serious note, Ashlyn has dealt with a loss. Not a normal loss, a profound loss that has changed her entire world. Her life has been turned upside down and she’s just trying to survive, pick up the pieces amongst all the changes. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/0e4ccc56-adda-405c-90a6-7c682d59f33f_zpsede3882e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1401425822i/9801334.jpg" alt=" photo 0e4ccc56-adda-405c-90a6-7c682d59f33f_zpsede3882e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>She’s starting her senior year off in a new place surrounded by strangers. On her way to her new place, she runs into a guy. A gorgeous guy who happens to grab her attention in a big way. <br><i>
  <blockquote>His eyes were so blue and filled with interest. For a second, I thought they were a passageway to a different world. <br>Beautiful.<br>  Breathtaking.<br>Brilliant.<br>Blue eyes. <br>I sighed. Maybe there were a passageway to a better world.</blockquote>
</i> When these two met and connected, I felt the world shift. They define the words ‘meant to be’. From the first time they hang out together, you can just tell. They have a deep connection. They have so much in common it’s uncanny. For the first time in a long time, Ashlyn feels something besides grief, sadness and anger. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“You know what I like about you so far?”<br><br>“What’s that?”<br><br> “Everything.”</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/d3809f11-769e-4c29-9d45-e4fff04b3bed_zpsc655357d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1401425822i/9801335.jpg" alt=" photo d3809f11-769e-4c29-9d45-e4fff04b3bed_zpsc655357d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Daniel makes her feel things she’s never felt. The texts, the letters, the Shakespeare. Things between them just click into place. Until Ashlyn’s first day of school, that is. Ashlyn struggles. With loving Daniel, and Mr. Daniels being her teacher. It takes her a while to see that they really are one in the same.<br><i>
  <blockquote>He was still there. Daniel wasn’t merely Mr. Daniels- he was still himself. And I was still on his mind, the same way he lived in mine. Maybe there weren’t two different Daniels. Maybe Mr. Daniels was just another part of him. So it wasn’t surprising that I had fallen for both sides of the coin. I was crazy about all of him- the good, the bad, and the broken pieces. I think I liked the broken pieces the most.</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/d0c1e020-bb9e-4a0a-ad7b-d483d1f647d0_zps1cbc7844.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1401425822i/9801336.jpg" alt=" photo d0c1e020-bb9e-4a0a-ad7b-d483d1f647d0_zps1cbc7844.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>“I think you’re beautiful. And I don’t mean your looks. I mean your smarts, your protectiveness, your brokenness. I think that’s beautiful.”<br><br> “I don’t want to be your friend. I want to be yours, I want you to be mine, and I hate that we can’t be us. Because I think we were meant to be us.” </blockquote>
</i><br>I could go on and on about this story all day, but it would be an injustice for me to try and retell any of the rest. It’s one you have to read for yourself. <br><br>Both characters are magnificent. I loved the Shakespeare ties between them. It was ‘their thing’. Daniel may be the most romantic and swoonworthy hero ever. He quotes poetry, he’s a musician, and he is just too sweet and lovable. Ashlyn was relatable. She was strong, brave and wonderful. They were both real. <br><br>And it wasn’t just the two of them that I loved. Some of the supporting characters were just as essential to the story as Ashlyn and Daniel were. Hailey, Ryan, even Gabby. Ryan stole my heart from the moment I met him. Favorite character of the book right there. <br><br><br>The love between Daniel and Ashlyn was powerful. It was beautiful and it was eternal. If you believe in people being soul mates, being meant to be, this couple will solidify that. If you don’t believe in that sort of thing, after reading LMD, you just might.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/43d959c8-dd9c-4ccd-b338-3deb8760a763_zpsb8dab35e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1401425822i/9801337.jpg" alt=" photo 43d959c8-dd9c-4ccd-b338-3deb8760a763_zpsb8dab35e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This story was so much more than just a romance between a student and a teacher. SO MUCH MORE. It’s a story of forgiveness, of healing, finding acceptance, following your dreams and following your heart. There were so many quotes that moved me.<br><i>
  <blockquote>“The best things in life aren’t easy. They are tough, they are painful, and they are raw. That makes the arrival to the final destination that much sweeter.” <br><br>“Pretending to be happy is almost like being happy. Until you remember that you’re only pretending. Then you’re sad. Really sad. Because wearing a mask every day of your life is the hardest thing to do. After a while, you get a little scared because the mask becomes you.”<br><br>“Humans weren’t made to be perfect, Daniel. We were made to screw up, fuck up, and learn new things. We were made perfectly imperfect.” <br><br>Maybe home wasn’t a location. Maybe it’s simply the people who you were surrounded with that make you feel as you could be whoever you wanted to be. Maybe home was friendship.</blockquote>
</i><br><br>I fell in love with this book. Completely and utterly in love. I was inspired and moved by what I read. The very best student/teacher book I’ve ever read. There were so many times I forgot it was a student/teacher book. I was so focused on the all consuming love between these two people. There was some conflict, but there was so much more to the story. There was a part of this story that gutted me. My cried and teared up more than once, but one scene in particular destroyed me. But I wasn’t in tears the entire time... I had a huge grin on my face for a lot of the book. The was laughter, tears and the feeling of a full heart once I’d finished. <br><br>LMD is one of the most beautiful stories I’ve ever read. It was <b>perfect, perfect.</b> The writing was out of this world. There were parts that reminded me of a Coleen Hoover book, and other parts that reminded me of a Jessica Park book (they are two of my favorite authors) and a lot of it was a style all of Ms. Cherry’s own. I just want everyone I know to pick this book up, read it, and come back to me and tell me how much you loved it too! It was a truly ‘GOLDEN’ read and one I can’t recommend enough! <br><i>
  <blockquote>“You’re the reason people believe in tomorrow. You’re the voice that scares the shadows away. You’re the love that makes me breathe.”</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/e96eb28a-cfc2-420b-842d-318f88b9ff18_zps924353ca.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1401425822i/9801338.jpg" alt=" photo e96eb28a-cfc2-420b-842d-318f88b9ff18_zps924353ca.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Our hearts would always beat for one another. Our souls were destined to burn together in a mystifying flame that lit with universe with hope and passion.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="14558057102783227303" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12790215067796482556"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451294389i/17525593.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451026167ra/17500381.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451250965ra/17520739.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451025593ra/17500324.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>★★★★! Loving Mr. Daniels (stand-alone). In the wake of tragedy two lost souls, one teacher, one student find solace & healing in each other!</b><br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I loved how distant we were but how close we felt.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/><b>Loving Mr. Daniel</b> (stand-alone) opens up to the aftermath of <b>Ashlyn Jennings</b> losing her best friend and twin sister to leukemia. Her mom ships her off to a small town to live with her estranged father and his new family. On the train she spots a handsome blue-eyed stranger who invite</span>
  <span id="freeText12790215067796482556" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451294389i/17525593.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451026167ra/17500381.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451250965ra/17520739.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451025593ra/17500324.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>★★★★! Loving Mr. Daniels (stand-alone). In the wake of tragedy two lost souls, one teacher, one student find solace &amp; healing in each other!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I loved how distant we were but how close we felt.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>Loving Mr. Daniel</b> (stand-alone) opens up to the aftermath of <b>Ashlyn Jennings</b> losing her best friend and twin sister to leukemia. Her mom ships her off to a small town to live with her estranged father and his new family. On the train she spots a handsome blue-eyed stranger who invites her to watch his band play. <br><br>They feel an instant attraction, but also as deeper kinship as both have tragic pasts neither has dealt with. After the concert they set a date, but before they can go out Ashlyn discovers that <b>Daniel Daniels</b> is her new English teacher, <b>Mr. Daniels.</b><br><br>Story follows them during the <b>school year</b> and into the future as they both cope with <b>life, loss, love, tragedy, healing and forgiveness.</b> All set against their forbidden friendship and a relationship that grows despite their better judgment.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I want to make love to you everywhere twice.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451294241ra/17525586.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Five words to describe <b>Daniel Daniels, Mr. Daniels: Charming, noble, patient, loyal and sweet</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451294241ra/17525587.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Five words to describe <b>Ashlyn Jennings: Broken, reflective observant, progressive and sweet</b>.<br><br><b>Loving Mr. Daniel</b> told from dual POVs, is a mixture of <b>coming of age, forbidden romance</b> and an <b>against-all-odds love.</b> Including epilogue, it spans years and was both ansty and sweet. <br><br><b>Poignant! Hopeful! Beautiful!</b> It’s a story I will remember.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I was the luckiest. Because for a moment he loved me back.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 4 stars <br>Heroine rating: 4 stars<br>Sexual tension rating: 4 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 4 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 4 stars<br>Plot rating: 5 stars<br>Dialogue rating: 4 stars<br>Storytelling rating: 5 stars<br>Story ending rating: 4 stars<br>************************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 4+ stars<br><br>Would I recommend this book: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this book: Maybe later.<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451385635ra/17536645.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_945485837" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945485837" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/945485837?book_show_action=true">May 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/30170064-loving-mr-daniels">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=forbidden-romance">forbidden-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=tearjerkers">tearjerkers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=sweet-heart-warming-stories">sweet-heart-warming-stories</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer945485837" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13011599304657724448">I love nothing like I love a taboo love story. So, it is no big surprise that this book had been sitting on my TBR for quite some time. Finally, I decided to download the audiobook and give it a listen. I am so glad that I did. This book was incredible!<br/><br/>First off, let me say that it was not the dirty, sordid affair that I had envisioned in my perverted mind. Yes, there is the obvious taboo nature of a student-teacher affair. However, it was almost easy to forget that that relationship dynamic exi</span>
  <span id="freeText13011599304657724448" style="display:none">I love nothing like I love a taboo love story. So, it is no big surprise that this book had been sitting on my TBR for quite some time. Finally, I decided to download the audiobook and give it a listen. I am so glad that I did. This book was incredible!<br /><br />First off, let me say that it was not the dirty, sordid affair that I had envisioned in my perverted mind. Yes, there is the obvious taboo nature of a student-teacher affair. However, it was almost easy to forget that that relationship dynamic existed. They just fit together so well, that there wasn't the obvious power differential that you'd expect in a student-teacher relationship. This was probably due, in part, to the fact that their ages were so close together.<br /> <br />In addition, Daniel, aka Mr. Daniels, actually meets Ashlyn outside of school without knowing that she was a student at the high school where he teaches. At only 22 years old, he might be the youngest high school teacher in history. Likewise, at 19 years old, Ashlyn is an anomaly as well. <br /><br />Needless to say, a 22 year-old and 19 year-old don't feel quite as taboo as a forty-something and an underage teen. So, as much as I love a naughty, salacious story, that wasn't what ended up being the draw for this story. It was just a sweet, heartwarming love story, with a touch of the forbidden.<br /><br />I don't want to give too much of this story away, but I will say that both of these characters had tons of baggage. They were both so broken, that it was difficult to watch. Finding each other was their saving grace. I don't think that anyone else would have been able to "get through" to either of these characters. It was meant to be.<br /><br />The supporting characters were also superb. I loved Hailey and Ryan. Even Ashlyn's deadbeat dad, Henry, won me over eventually. The backstories were engaging and enlightening, helping to move things along and highlight significant facets of their lives.<br /><br />There isn't anything that I'd change about this story. It made me cry. It made me smile. The narration was fabulous. I couldn't have found a better standalone story to pass the time. I loved every minute of this book!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13011599304657724448" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1465539648" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1465539648" />
    <a title="Cristina Monica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica"><img alt="Cristina Monica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589617514p2/14596170.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1465539648?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cristina Monica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cristina Monica" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica">Cristina Monica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=death">death</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=high-school">high-school</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1465539648" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2882954745512445268"> <strong>So cheesy… yet so PERFECTLY ADORABLE.</strong><br/><br/> I’m really not the type of person who swoons when reading corny romance stories, but student-teacher relationships have always been a turn on for me. So I guess I didn’t mind the cheesiness, since it wasn’t the only thing we were exposed to.<br/><br/> Ashlyn and Mr. Daniels’ story is so freaking cute. They meet in a train, by pure coincidence, and they’re immediately attracted to one another. <strong>ALRIGHT</strong>, so that’s not the best way to start a love story (insta-lust), in </span>
  <span id="freeText2882954745512445268" style="display:none"> <strong>So cheesy… yet so PERFECTLY ADORABLE.</strong><br /><br /> I’m really not the type of person who swoons when reading corny romance stories, but student-teacher relationships have always been a turn on for me. So I guess I didn’t mind the cheesiness, since it wasn’t the only thing we were exposed to.<br /><br /> Ashlyn and Mr. Daniels’ story is so freaking cute. They meet in a train, by pure coincidence, and they’re immediately attracted to one another. <strong>ALRIGHT</strong>, so that’s not the best way to start a love story (insta-lust), in my opinion, and I’m disappointed to see how the author couldn’t think of anything else to be the starting point of their relationship… but it’s okay. Not great, but okay.<br /><br /> Then they see each other for the second time in a bar, because – wait for it – Daniel is a singer! Yes, you heard me. Of course he had to be a singer. I hate singers. I mean… I hate love stories with singers who fall in love with non-singer girls or guys. For me, it’s the most cliché thing on this planet. I’m tired of it. So that’s mainly why this book loses a couple of points from me.<br /><br /> Everything from that point on – after she hears Daniel play and learns he’s her new teacher – is a <strong>delight to read</strong>! While I didn’t like the idea of Daniel also being a singer (although not extremely famous), I did enjoy reading the snippets of lyrics that are written at the beginning of every new chapter. I know it’s strange to like the songs but not the <em>singers</em> themselves, but I guess – hope – we all have our book-related turn offs. Plus I really, really liked Daniel’s sweet soul… just not his singer side.<br /><br /> You will be surprised, when starting the story, to see how much this book deals with death. The theme is there at the beginning and keeps on being present until the very last page. There’s something like four people who die, and while I thought this to be a bit of an exaggeration from the author’s part, I just went along with the whole drama. It’s dramatic, and sometimes <em>overdramatic</em>, but I’ve always liked intensity in books.<br /><br /> Another thing you’ll quickly notice is how fast and easily this story reads. It’s just such a relaxing, calm (despite all the telenovela-worthy elements) and wonderful read. <strong><em>Loving Mr. Daniels</em> beautifully defines what it means to love someone… and why it’s important to let them go.</strong> Unlike what I first thought, the plot doesn’t revolve around Ashlyn and Daniel’s fear of being discovered, although they’re being extremely careful for that exact reason. No, the author didn’t want that to distract us from what’s most important: Ashlyn’s struggling to deal with the death of her twin sister, building a relationship with her stranger of a dad and unfolding Mr. Daniels.<br /><br /> You don’t even need my recommendation to read this book if you’re a lover of new adult intense romances easy to dive into and with characters that we wish were real. Happy reading!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2882954745512445268" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_915786430" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/915786430" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/915786430?book_show_action=true">Apr 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer915786430" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17074780754868424841"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400057356i/9628893._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Ohhh I loved this one!!!! “Love loved” it actually. And yes, that’s a double ;) </b><br/><br/>This beautiful story was so much more than a romance. It took me by surprise in the best of ways. It was a love story and it was a life story. All kinds of love, all kinds of life. I laughed, I cried and I totally felt it!!<br/><br/>The first thing that drew me to this story was the blurb. My heart was racing from the moment I came across it and I just knew this was a book I had read…<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>To Whom it May Concern, <br/><br/>It was easy to c</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText17074780754868424841" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400057356i/9628893._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Ohhh I loved this one!!!! “Love loved” it actually. And yes, that’s a double ;) </b><br><br>This beautiful story was so much more than a romance. It took me by surprise in the best of ways. It was a love story and it was a life story. All kinds of love, all kinds of life. I laughed, I cried and I totally felt it!!<br><br>The first thing that drew me to this story was the blurb. My heart was racing from the moment I came across it and I just knew this was a book I had read…<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>To Whom it May Concern, <br><br>It was easy to call us forbidden and harder to call us soulmates. Yet I believed we were both. Forbidden soulmates. <br><br>When I arrived to Edgewood, Wisconsin I didn’t plan to find him. I didn’t plan to stumble into Joe’s bar and have Daniel’s music stir up my emotions. I had no clue that his voice would make my hurts forget their own sorrow. I had no idea that my happiness would remember its own bliss. <br><br>When I started senior year at my new school, I wasn’t prepared to call him Mr. Daniels, but sometimes life happens at the wrong time for all the right reasons. <br><br>Our love story wasn’t only about the physical connection. <br><br>It was about family. It was about loss. It was about being alive. It was silly. It was painful. It was mourning. It was laughter. <br><br>It was ours. <br><br>And for those reasons alone, I would never apologize for loving Mr. Daniels. <br><br>-Ashlyn Jennings</i>
</blockquote><br><br>So I thought I knew what to expect from this book — a forbidden student-teacher romance, right? — but what I got from this story went above and beyond my every expectation. It surprised me, thrilled me, captivated me. It made me swoon, it made me cry, it made me laugh. It took me on an absolutely unforgettable journey.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I don’t want to be your friend… I want to be yours, I want you to be mine, and I hate that we can’t be us. Because I think we were meant to be us.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The main story follows Ashlyn — a 19 year-old student who had just lost her beloved twin sister to cancer. Reeling from the loss, she’s further devastated when her mother sends her to Wisconsin to live with her estranged father and his new family. On the train, she meets a guy — a 22-year-old gorgeous, blue-eyed musician who she later goes to see perform….<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I couldn’t believe that girl deserved to be so sad. I secretly hoped that someday someone could make her smile… I hoped someday she would be all right.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>They have this beautiful, intense connection, this breathless spark between them which is shaken on the day they both walk into class… her as a student, him as her teacher.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Was I dating my English teacher? Was what we were doing truly unethical? Falling in love? Could falling in love ever be wrong?” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The conflict of their situation gave me butterflies. It was thrilling and heart-wrenching all at the same time. Their relationship was completely forbidden, yet having what they could never indulge in right in front of them each day was just consuming them. I think this was one of my favorite quotes from Daniel that perfectly described what they were going through…<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I hated that I couldn’t tell her how beautiful she looked each and every day. I hated that, when she walked into my classroom, I had to pretend that she wasn’t on my mind…. I hated how close we were but how distant we felt.”<br><br>“I loved how beautiful she looked each and every day. I loved that, when she walked into my classroom, she was on my mind…. I loved how distant we were but how close we felt.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Gosh, how beautiful is that??<br><br>But this is about so much more than just a romance. So much more!!!! When Ashlyn moves in with her father’s family, she becomes close with the two teenage children of the woman he was living with. Each of them are so different and yet they’re each hiding pain behind their masks of happiness and despite their differences, they all quickly form a very tight bond. Hailey was a hoot (I loved her!!) but the poor girl was searching for happiness in all the wrong places. And Ryan just made my heart squeeze. I don’t want to say too much but his pain went so deep that even thinking about it now makes me choked up.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I was lost, but so were they. <br>There were no maps to be found. <br>At least I wasn’t walking alone.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Not only were the siblings Hailey and Ryan a central part of the story, but the author found an absolutely beautiful way to incorporate Ashlyn’s twin, Gabby, into her life even though she wasn’t physically there. More than once, the deeply moving notes she’d left behind brought tears to my eyes and I’d want to stop and read them twice just to re-experience their beauty.<br><br>The supporting characters played such a vital role in this book. I really felt like it was as much their story as it was Ashlyn and Daniel’s. Their journeys complimented the story. brought an added depth to it, and left us with some very profound messages that I think will resonate with a lot of people.<br><br>I loved the whole emotional spectrum that this book made me experience as the story progressed through first love, sibling bonds, new friendships, healing families, coming of age, finding oneself, living dreams … all of it just came together in a way I couldn’t help but feel deep down in my heart.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Daniel,” I whispered… “You’re doing it.”<br>“Doing what?”<br>“Bringing me back to life.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Even just thinking back on the story brings a smile to my face and makes my heart both ache and feel full at the same time. I truly loved it but in the interest of full honesty, I’ll say that it wasn’t perfect for me. As I read, I felt myself fall in love with the story but then there’d be moments (more in the first half of the book) when I’d drift away from my connection a little, only to then be drawn back in … and I did make note of a few things that bothered me while I was reading but now that I’ve finished my read and I’m looking back on it, the only things that stand out to me are the positive things that I loved so I’m just going to say that while this book wasn’t perfect, I still completely loved it and highly recommend it for everyone.<br><br>This is the kind of story that stays in your heart long after you’ve finished reading it. Brittainy C. Cherry has written a stunning novel and I can’t wait to see what she has in store for us next!<br><br><b>Rating: 4.5+ stars. Standalone New Adult Romance. </b><br><i>Recommended for fans of Slammed by Colleen Hoover. </i><br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="17074780754868424841" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1719132715" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1719132715" />
    <a title="Maria✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44673856-maria-steamy-reads-blog"><img alt="Maria✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484605631p2/44673856.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1719132715?book_show_action=true">Aug 04, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maria✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maria✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦" href="/user/show/44673856-maria-steamy-reads-blog">Maria✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44673856-maria-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=student-teacher">student-teacher</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44673856-maria-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44673856-maria-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=taboo">taboo</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1719132715" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3458507311451459425"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466194304i/19451974.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1470679218i/19952568._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I’ve never seen two people who loved each other so quietly."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466042213i/19431593.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>➦This is a <b>forbidden romance</b> between a <b>teacher and a student.</b> The main characters meet before they realize they are a teacher/student and make a connection. Needless to say they are bummed out once this fact is revealed. And so they fight the temptation. <br/><br/>❤This novel is about <b>loss and love.</b> I loved that the mcs connected through their <b>love of poetry.</b> This novel kind of reminded me of Amy Harmon's <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29698573.A_Different_Blue' title='A Different Blue by Amy Harmon' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1459259221s/29698573.jpg' alt='A Different Blue by Amy Harmon' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> with the whole poetry q</span>
  <span id="freeText3458507311451459425" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466194304i/19451974.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1470679218i/19952568._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I’ve never seen two people who loved each other so quietly."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466042213i/19431593.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>➦This is a <b>forbidden romance</b> between a <b>teacher and a student.</b> The main characters meet before they realize they are a teacher/student and make a connection. Needless to say they are bummed out once this fact is revealed. And so they fight the temptation. <br><br>❤This novel is about <b>loss and love.</b> I loved that the mcs connected through their <b>love of poetry.</b> This novel kind of reminded me of Amy Harmon's <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29698573.A_Different_Blue" title="A Different Blue by Amy Harmon" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1459259221s/29698573.jpg" alt="A Different Blue by Amy Harmon" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> with the whole poetry quoting that was going on here. The book is <b>romantic</b> and even steamy at times. <br><br>✘If I were to point out one thing I didn't like it would be the tone of the book. It was very... well, <b> gloomy.</b> It also touched on a lot of sensitive subjects, like <b>death, alcoholism, repressed homosexuality.</b> There's <b>whole lot of death</b> in this book and I thought it was a bit of an overkill. <br><br>➦I recommend this book to those who enjoy <b>forbidden romances</b>, books with an emphasis on <b>poetry and music. </b><br><br>➦Side note: this is my second book by Brittainy C. Cherry and, even though her first novel was a complete miss for me, I've <b>enjoyed this one</b> a lot. Her books do seem to be kind of on a heavy, <b>depressing</b> side. Looking forward to reading more in the future.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466174176i/19449322.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/SteamyReadsBlog/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473872687i/20525702.jpg" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow us on facebook" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.instagram.com/steamyreads/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473872687i/20525703.jpg" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow us on instagram" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.steamyreads.net" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473872687i/20525705.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_929433397" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/929433397" />
    <a title="Patrycja" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja"><img alt="Patrycja" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586460589p2/6852653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/929433397?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patrycja" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patrycja" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja">Patrycja</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=arc-s">arc-s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=must-read">must-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer929433397" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2556122541213454860"><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Title:</b> Loving Mr Daniels<br/><b>Series:</b> No<br/><b>Author:</b> Brittainy C Cherry<br/><b>Release Date: </b> May 13, 2014<br/><b>Rating:</b> 5 ++ stars<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b>No<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Yes  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>☆ 5 GOLDEN STARS ☆ </b><br/><br/><i>
  <b>“When hearts are set on fire no complications can extinguish the flames”</b>
</i><br/><br/><i>Loving Mr Daniels</i> by Brittainy C. Cherry is completely amazing, touching and exceptional bittersweet tale of love, life and moving on. It’s a book that touches the subject of unconditional love and asks important questions, only to answer them</span>
  <span id="freeText2556122541213454860" style="display:none"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b> Loving Mr Daniels<br><b>Series:</b> No<br><b>Author:</b> Brittainy C Cherry<br><b>Release Date: </b> May 13, 2014<br><b>Rating:</b> 5 ++ stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b>No<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>☆ 5 GOLDEN STARS ☆ </b><br><br><i>
  <b>“When hearts are set on fire no complications can extinguish the flames”</b>
</i><br><br><i>Loving Mr Daniels</i> by Brittainy C. Cherry is completely amazing, touching and exceptional bittersweet tale of love, life and moving on. It’s a book that touches the subject of unconditional love and asks important questions, only to answer them in the most beautiful way –no, it doesn’t give away simple responses, it makes you think and feel. And that what’s counts the most. <br> <br>What a wonderful story! I’m wowed. I’m swept of my feet.<b> I’m totally, entirely, wholly, utterly, absolutely in love with this magical, heartbreaking tale of forbidden love</b>. There are really no words to summarize how I felt while reading this novel, this book is just one of those that grab your soul, heart and mind and don’t let go; this is a story that will stay with me for quite some time and I am so sad, I reached the ending so quickly. <br><br><i>
  <b>“The best things in life aren't easy. They are tough, they are painful, and they are raw. That makes the arrival to the final destination that much sweeter."</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399742378i/9590646._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ashlyn is depressed, lonely and lost nineteen year old young woman who just lost her twin sister. Gabrielle was her best friend, her better part, her soul mate, her confidante. Now, after she died, Ashlyn is all alone. Her mother sent her to live with her dad, who she almost doesn’t know. Wisconsin seems like a very distant place and Ashlyn has one more year of high school to go through.<br><br>Daniel is as much broken and lost as Ashlyn. Although he’s sexy, intelligent and a good man, he’s also living in the world where everything is marked by pain and grief. He lost his mother and father; his younger brother is more trouble than you can think. And even being a lead singer of Romeo Quest or teaching English doesn’t soothe his tortured soul. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399742378i/9590647.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When Daniel and Ashlyn meet in train to Wisconsin and quickly learn they share the same passion for Shakespeare’s work, something inside them clicks. It’s like a new beginning for both of them. It’s the start of something beautiful yet forbidden. <br><br><b>
  <i>"There had been one moment when I saw someone who might understand, based solely on her eyes. Her eyes were surreal, haunting even. Green, powerful eyes that looked so sad. Broken. Beautiful."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399742378i/9590648.jpg" width="400" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So strong, so powerful and so intense - <i>Loving Mr Daniels</i> is not average forbidden love story. This student/teacher relationship is in no means your usual dose of angst and typical problems and issues we generally get in this type of romances. It’s so much more. <br> <br>From the complex characters that won me over to heartbreaking storyline Brittainy C. Cherry astounded me. I loved everything that was the part of this novel, and that rarely happens these days. Even secondary characters were perfect addition to it. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399742378i/9590649.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Loving Mr Daniels</i> is breathtaking, thrilling, sometimes overwhelming and gutting read and I loved every minute of it. This is a book that is not only worth reading, but is worth writing about, talking about it and recommending to your best friend. This is unforgettable tale of love I will carry close to my heart forever. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399742378i/9590650.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>ARC provided by author in exchange for honest review </b>
</i><br><br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT BOOK BLOG ON: <b><br><br><a href="https://twitter.com/BlogSmokin/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Twitter" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391768351i/8452934.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="http://facebook.com/smokinhotbookblog" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Smokin Hot Book Blog" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391769122i/8453144.png" width="32" height="32"         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer939760491" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12569714732199850118"><a href='http://imgur.com/DfaBiz6' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400452384ra/9677931.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>Yes, I am fully aware that I will be in the minority, but I don't care. I must speak my peace. <br/><b> (WARNING: SPOILERS BELOW.) Things I couldn't stand</b><br/><i> Note: I already know how bitchy this is all going to sound. WHAT FOLLOWS IS A RANT...</i><br/>1) 2%-32% on my Kindle was Ashlynn. And then, out of nowhere, Daniel's POV comes out of hiding and a nice flow of one chapter Ashlynn, the next chapter Daniel, forms. I didn't like that. I'd gotten comfortable with Ashlynn's POV, so when his popped up I was a litt</span>
  <span id="freeText12569714732199850118" style="display:none"><a href="http://imgur.com/DfaBiz6" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400452384ra/9677931.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Yes, I am fully aware that I will be in the minority, but I don't care. I must speak my peace. <br><b> (WARNING: SPOILERS BELOW.) Things I couldn't stand</b><br><i> Note: I already know how bitchy this is all going to sound. WHAT FOLLOWS IS A RANT...</i><br>1) 2%-32% on my Kindle was Ashlynn. And then, out of nowhere, Daniel's POV comes out of hiding and a nice flow of one chapter Ashlynn, the next chapter Daniel, forms. I didn't like that. I'd gotten comfortable with Ashlynn's POV, so when his popped up I was a little disappointed. <br><br>2) There is a dead epidemic going on:<br>Daniel's mother: Dead.<br>Daniel's father: Dead.<br>Daniel's former girlfriend, Sarah: Dead.<br>Ashlynn's twin sister: Dead.<br>Randy's parents and sister: Dead.<br><br>3) Too many quotes by Shakes. We get it, they're obsessed with literature. But no man, I don't care how <i>romantic</i> he is, is going to quote Shakes before going down on a woman. And if he did, I would be questioning what the hell was wrong with him. <br><br>4) Ashlynn pity party. Apparently she's the only one hurting and because of that she can lash out at anyone she wants, including: Rebecca, Henry ect...No. I found it hard to like her during certain chapters and I'm still not convinced that she's this "sweet girl".<br><br>5) The letters from Gabby. (Been there, read that.) I was reminded of A Walk to Remember, when Landon started fulfilling Jamie's list. When Daniel kissed Ashlynn in the bar, I thought of Landon. When Ashlynn saw Daniel at the cemetary and they got all cozy, I thought of Landon and Jamie searching for stars at the cemetary. <br><a href="http://imgur.com/uCkcw2W" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400452384ra/9677932.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://imgur.com/eloJuBb" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400452384ra/9677933.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>6) Ryan dies at 73%. What was the purpose of this, exactly? I don't know. To add more drama?<br><br>7) I don't buy for a second that Ashlynn had never had an orgasm before Daniel came along. Not with the way she touched herself in his Jeep.<br><br>8) The sex scenes were never played out fully, except for one. I don't know what people consider this book to be (Erotica, New Adult, Romance ect) but it is definitely not Erotica. <br><br>9) Constantly pointing out the obvious. For example: She see's the cereal and marshmallows on the table. "You got me Cap'n Crunch and added marshmallows?" or She saw the letter lying on the bed. "You read my letter?!!!" (There was too much repetetiveness.) <br><br>10) The word <i>perfectly imperfect.</i> If I read this word 50 years from now, it would still be too soon. Every time <i>perfectly imperfect</i> popped up on my kindle, I thought of Demi Lovato, Joe Jonas, and that damn Camp Rock song that played a few summers ago.<br>Insert chord from "Wouldn't Change a Thing" by Demi and Joe. <br><b> We're perfectly imperfect, but I wouldn't change a thing....</b> *ORCHESTRA FINGERS* Everybody sing the chorus...in 1...2....3<br><a href="http://imgur.com/GzmeLWS" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400452384ra/9677934.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>11) Ryan dies and all Ashlynn can think of is Daniel and her twin. It's like Ryan never existed. There is no mourning on her end, nothing. One would think it's because she's "shed too many tears" but I thought it was just laziness. She can cry over Daniel not texting her, but she can't mourn over Ryan taking his own life. (2 pages isn't mourning.)<br><a href="http://imgur.com/Y7YrSak" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400452384ra/9677935.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>12) Ashlynn, Ashlynn, Ashlynn. It was all about Ashlynn all the time. Screw the fact that Daniel lost his entire family (except for his brother). She's <i>that</i> kind of person. The one who, no matter what you've been through, she's been through worse. <br>Example: If someone were to say "I've had a kidney stone" Ashlynn would say something like "Well I was sick when I was younger and got held back..."<br>She's just not likable at all.<br><a href="http://imgur.com/pEpSQr3" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400452384ra/9677936.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>13) All anyone did in this book was cry. You can't make it through one chapter without Ashlynn crying for some reason. Even something as petty as people whispering about her. Really? Sooo damn frustrating.<br><a href="http://imgur.com/TIpiZEv" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400452384ra/9677937.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i> He would come; I knew he would. If Daniel Daniel's loved me the way I knew he did, he would show up.<br>"I'm sad." I said breathily</i> Oh please....She acts like a 4-year-old!<br><a href="http://imgur.com/Lj8ryt5" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400452384ra/9677938.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>"Twisted" fans, (aka Emma Chase fans) would probably like this. Ashlynn pulls a Kate at the end and throws out a "I want to be on my own to prove I can do it." <br>There is so much back and forth in this book from both Ashlynn and Daniel. They broke up like 4 or 5 times throughout this and I honestly don't know how that appeals to people lol. If you're not ready to have your character commit, then hold off using the word "Boyfriend" for a while. Don't make it exclusive! Easy fix, there ya go!<br><a href="http://imgur.com/pxrd0Gu" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400200067ra/9647904.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>So Ashlynn leaves to find herself...Right at the 90% mark in my Kindle. Three years pass by in 6 pages. Enter: RUSHED ENDING. Ladies, she was gone for a total of 8 pages. <br><a href="http://imgur.com/juAyOqr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400452384ra/9677939.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Conclusion: 2 stars. (Reasons are listed above...)<br>I can't find it in me to like this book or hate it entirely. At times the Shakes quotes were sweet, and then just stupid. We never heard much about his ex-girlfriend Sarah, whom Daniel had confessed he would still be with had she not passed. That story was just tossed to the side and left unfinished. We don't know what happened to Bentley. Did he finally move on? What's going on there? I briefly thought Hailey and Randy had a connection at the funeral, but it was over as fast as it started. Did she finally make peace with Ryan's death? And most importantly, what about Rebecca? TOO MANY OPEN DOORS. <br>In the end, Ashlynn was a hypocrite. She did exactly what her mother did to her. She ran away (to California) and blocked everyone out. <br>So no, I don't really like this book. I'm not sure if it's because the ending was tied in a pretty white bow or...It just wasn't my thing. <br><a href="http://imgur.com/vapJFQf" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400452384ra/9677940.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12569714732199850118" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer1614609967523764258">It's LIVE......<a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.amazon.com/dp/B00K9V2OPE/ref=cm_sw_su_dp'>http://www.amazon.com/dp/B00K9V2OPE/r...</a><br/><br/>5+++ <b>Beautiful Beautiful</b> Stars!!!<br/><br/><b>Ashlyn</b><br/><br/>A woman drowning in her sorrows. Barely floating on the surface after the death of her twin sister. Abandoned by the person she loved the most. Sent to live with a stranger. <br/><br/><b>Gabrielle</b><br/><br/>Fought and lost her battle with cancer. A tragedy that tore a family apart. A loss that brought two people together. A treasure box of memories and letters that would eventually heal.<br/> <br/><b>Daniel</b><br/><br/>A man drowning in his sorrows. Ba</span>
  <span id="freeText1614609967523764258" style="display:none">It's LIVE......<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/dp/B00K9V2OPE/ref=cm_sw_su_dp">http://www.amazon.com/dp/B00K9V2OPE/r...</a><br><br>5+++ <b>Beautiful Beautiful</b> Stars!!!<br><br><b>Ashlyn</b><br><br>A woman drowning in her sorrows. Barely floating on the surface after the death of her twin sister. Abandoned by the person she loved the most. Sent to live with a stranger. <br><br><b>Gabrielle</b><br><br>Fought and lost her battle with cancer. A tragedy that tore a family apart. A loss that brought two people together. A treasure box of memories and letters that would eventually heal.<br> <br><b>Daniel</b><br><br>A man drowning in his sorrows. Barely floating on the surface after the death of his mother and father. Betrayed by his family. Trying to move on, to start over.<br><br>A chance meeting at the train station...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"Beautiful.<br>Breathtaking.<br>Brilliant. <br>Blue eyes."</blockquote>
</b><br>Two people, one night...his music awakened something in her that had been laid to rest. A shared love for Shakespeare...two lost souls, who found each other. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399324279i/9535063.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"If there was a God, which I'm not certain there is, do you think this night would be a form of apology for him taking away the things we loved?"</blockquote>
</b><br>New school. New friendships. A new life. <br><br>A teacher. A student. A forbidden love.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"He wasn't the handsome man who'd awakened my spirits a few nights ago with his romantic vocals. He wasn't the man who'd made me laugh and allowed me to cry into him. He wasn't the man who'd reminded me that I was still alive when his lips had triumphantly found mine. No, he wasn't Daniel anymore. He was Mr. Daniels."</blockquote>
</b><br>Daniel. Ashlyn. Ryan. Hailey. Four people living a lie. Loving the wrong people. Believing in the wrong things. Craving acceptance. Weighed down by past sorrows. Hoping. Dreaming. Wishing. Craving. Acceptance. Love. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401176ra/778336.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"Because pretending to be happy is almost like being happy. Until you remember that you're only pretending. Then you're sad. Really sad. Because wearing a mask every day of your life is the hardest thing to do. And after a while, you get a little scared because the mask becomes you."</blockquote>
</b><br>A secret affair. Stolen moments. Innocent looks. Hidden touches. <br> <br><b>
  <blockquote>"I hated how close we were but how distant we felt.<br>I loved how distant we were but how close we felt."</blockquote>
</b><br>Sacrificing their love in order to protect each other. Willing to let each other go to save themselves. Giving up today so that they might be able to have a tomorrow. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398262248ra/9392651.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"I want to be yours, I want you to be mine, and I hate that we can't be us. Because I think we were meant to be us."</blockquote>
</b><br>A once in a life-time love. A forever love. <br><b>
  <blockquote>"I love you slowly...<br>I love you deeply.<br>I love you quietly.<br>I love you powerfully. <br>I love you undconditionally.<br>I love you gently and hard, slow and fast. Before time and after.<br>I love you because I was born to do so."</blockquote>
</b><br>Ashlyn and Daniel. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390341070ra/8194426.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Absolutely beautiful-beautiful, heartbreaking-heartbreaking, breathtaking-breathtaking. I fell in love with every character in this book, not just Ashlyn and Daniel. This was a wonderful story of loss, healing, forgiveness, the power of friendship and above all else a great love. <br><br><b>ARC kindly provided by the author in exchange for an honest review</b></span>

<div id="review_924479466" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/924479466" />
    <a title="Lucia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia"><img alt="Lucia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484242793p2/8837962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/924479466?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucia" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia">Lucia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=5-stars-read">5-stars-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer924479466" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4987368818411857692"><blockquote>
  <b>* Beautiful - Unforgettable - Touching *</b>
</blockquote><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399650048i/9578687._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I have a soft spot for teacher/student romances. But a simple fact that author tells a story of forbidden love between teacher and student is no guarantee that I will enjoy it. However, this novel made a huge impression on me. Loving Mr. Daniels is <b>beautiful, complex</b> and <b>powerful</b> story that talks about life destinies of multiple people, story that I will remember forever! <br/><blockquote>
  <i>"I was convinced that everyone in the world had a form of weirdness to them. T</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText4987368818411857692" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>* Beautiful - Unforgettable - Touching *</b>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399650048i/9578687._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have a soft spot for teacher/student romances. But a simple fact that author tells a story of forbidden love between teacher and student is no guarantee that I will enjoy it. However, this novel made a huge impression on me. Loving Mr. Daniels is <b>beautiful, complex</b> and <b>powerful</b> story that talks about life destinies of multiple people, story that I will remember forever! <br><blockquote>
  <i>"I was convinced that everyone in the world had a form of weirdness to them. The idea of finding your other weirdo was so attractive to me."</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399650048i/9578688.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>With shocking prologue and emotional first chapter, author managed to hook me into the story pretty easily and since than I couldn’t put the book down. So what is so special about this novel? Sometimes it is writing style that grabs your attention. In other cases, it may be a storyline. Or feelings that book evokes in you. This book has it all.</b><br><br>Miserable. That’s how our 19 years old heroine <i>Ashlyn</i> feels at the beginning of this novel. Devastated by her twin’s death, hurt because of her broken relationship with her mum, angry because she is forced to move in with her dad and his other family in different town to finish high school. Not the best outlook for a teenage girl, right? Can attractive musician Daniel she meets on train be her saving grace?<br><br><i>Daniel</i> was perfect mix of nerdy and sexy young man. However, living in his own world of grief, there was a lot of misery in the life of Daniel Daniels. Connected by emotional pain and loneliness, a huge spark was ignited when Daniel and Ashlyn got to know each other one fateful night. If only they knew that what they felt that night would quickly become forbidden... <br><br><i>What happens when you meet your other half at really wrong time of your life?</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399650048i/9578689.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I could write really long list of reasons why I loved this book but I’m going to mention just couple of them in this review. I absolutely adored Ashlyn’s way of thinking and parts written in her POV. There was no over-the-top drama, just plenty of realistic emotions that were pouring out of this novel at every page, making me completely immersed into Ashlyn’s and Daniel’s life stories. Moreover, author created unique and unforgettable characters. Main or supporting ones, alive or dead, everyone played important role and touched me deeply in one way or another. <br><br>Ashlyn and Daniel were so "perfectly imperfect" together. Sharing all those nerdy quirks made them such an adorable and lovable couple for me, that I was rooting for them despite the fact that it was "forbidden". All I can say is that you need to experience this exceptional connection and love between those two people yourself. <b>For me, Loving Mr. Daniels is a definite must-read!</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399650048i/9578690.jpg" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><i>*ARC provided by author as an exchange for honest review*</i><br><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Reading Is My Breathing</b>
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="4987368818411857692" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/936870602" />
    <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake"><img alt="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605987751p2/11626803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/936870602?book_show_action=true">May 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake">Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=young-adult-new-adult">young-adult-new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=2-stars">2-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer936870602" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17905611972014724176">I am totally in the minority on this one, but I just didn't really like this... <br/><br/>I felt like someone took <i>PS I Love You, A Walk to Remember, Until November, Slammed</i>, and some random YA cliches and threw them all in a blender together and hit the "smoothie" button.<br/><br/>Plus, I think it was just too sappy and over the top in the cutesy department for my tastes.<br/><br/>***Spoilers Ahead***<br/><br/>But mostly, I felt that there was death overkill. <br/><br/>Ashlyn's twin died. <br/>Daniel's mother is murdered...<br/>His Dad dies...<br/>For shit's</span>
  <span id="freeText17905611972014724176" style="display:none">I am totally in the minority on this one, but I just didn't really like this... <br /><br />I felt like someone took <i>PS I Love You, A Walk to Remember, Until November, Slammed</i>, and some random YA cliches and threw them all in a blender together and hit the "smoothie" button.<br /><br />Plus, I think it was just too sappy and over the top in the cutesy department for my tastes.<br /><br />***Spoilers Ahead***<br /><br />But mostly, I felt that there was death overkill. <br /><br />Ashlyn's twin died. <br />Daniel's mother is murdered...<br />His Dad dies...<br />For shit's sake, even the poor guy's first girlfriend died. <br />Hailey and Ryan's Dad also dies. <br /><br />All from awful disease or tragic accident. <br /><br />And then Ryan dies too?! <br /><br />Seriously?!?!?!?! *face palm*<br /><br />This author should write for Sons of Anarchy or Game of Thrones since she likes to kill everyone off. Either that or she was trying to create drama and character complexity through the old death plot device short cut. When in doubt, kill someone off!<br /><br />I don't know, it just seemed like overkill (pun absolutely intended) to me and I just didn't buy it.</span>
