<div id="review_1160142560" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1160142560" />
    <a title="Aj the Ravenous Reader" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader"><img alt="Aj the Ravenous Reader" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557800982p2/30248594.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1160142560?book_show_action=true">Jan 07, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aj the Ravenous Reader" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aj the Ravenous Reader" href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader">Aj the Ravenous Reader</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=definitely-not-young-adult">definitely-not-young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=reality-bites">reality-bites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1160142560" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3131517783809682504"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425526642i/13902332.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i> <b> “You know those people you could go years without seeing and when you finally get together it felt like no time had passed? Hold on to those people. “ </b></i> <br/><br/>Sometimes, the simplest book titles will give you the most brilliant stories. This book did exactly just that. <3 <3 <3 <br/><br/>This book is an intricate quilt of wonderfully weaved stories about grief, death, friendship, coming to terms with one’s identity, broken families, life and love of genuine and lovable characters who will tremendously affect y</span>
  <span id="freeText3131517783809682504" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425526642i/13902332.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> <b> “You know those people you could go years without seeing and when you finally get together it felt like no time had passed? Hold on to those people. “ </b></i> <br><br>Sometimes, the simplest book titles will give you the most brilliant stories. This book did exactly just that. &lt;3 &lt;3 &lt;3 <br><br>This book is an intricate quilt of wonderfully weaved stories about grief, death, friendship, coming to terms with one’s identity, broken families, life and love of genuine and lovable characters who will tremendously affect you whether you like it or not. <br><br>The ingenuity of the author is evident in the way she skillfully plotted the story which is basically anchored at Gabby’s bucket list for Ashlyn. Gabby, Ashlyn’s twin sister died of leukemia but before she passed away, she left Ashlyn a bucket list. It is now up to Ashlyn to live life not only for herself but for Gabby as well through the list Gabby dedicatedly and painstakingly made for her sister. *Sniffs*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1409055084ra/10927422.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> For every item in the list that Ashlyn strikes off, she gets to read a letter from her twin sister. In other cases, the third party involved (say a stranger Ashlyn kissed) gets to read the letter. *Sniffs more* <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392981040ra/8642441.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This clearly shows that a loved one may be gone but their influence in our lives will forever linger. In this case, Gabby is the reason Ashlyn’s life will never be the same again. That Ashlyn despite the grief, bullying and rejection she went through still has a shot and hope at the brighter side of life. <br><br>The pivotal point of the plot is the entrance of Mr. Daniels in the picture. Who he is and what his role is in the story is up to you to find out. Don't rely too much on the blurb- that I can tell you. ^^<br><br><i> <b> ”His eyes were so blue and filled with interest. For a second, I thought they were a passage way to a different world." </b></i> <br><br>Ms. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7121791.Brittainy_C__Cherry" title="Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">Brittainy Cherry</a> is a magnificent writer for making this book seem to be a collaborative work of Colleen Hoover and John Green! <br><br><b> The witty and funny undertones… </b><br><br> <i> "He was so smart that he made me want to crawl into his head and live there." </i><br><br><b> the cleverness of the characters… </b><br><br><i> “There was nothing as romantic as the feel of book in your hands." </i><br><br><b> the romantic air that filled the entire story (especially with the allusions to Shakespeare)… </b><br><br><i> "You deserve to be the chorus to a person’s favorite song. You deserve to be the dedication in their favorite book." </i> <br><br><b> …easily flow along the pages of the book. The metaphors either make effortless connection to your heart or they could easily make your knees wobbly. </b><br><br><i> “His kisses tasted like forever soaked in always” </i><br><br>I have never been a huge fan of the NA genre but this is one of the most ultimate exceptions. Read this book and learn to mourn and celebrate life, to grieve and be just you with someone who completely understands. Read this <b> <i> imperfectly perfect </i></b>  book and be inspired!<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3131517783809682504" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_3551334080" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3551334080" />
    <a title="Mali Mor ❤️ The Romantic Blogger" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/88472183-mali-mor-the-romantic-blogger"><img alt="Mali Mor ❤️ The Romantic Blogger" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1560790165p2/88472183.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3551334080?book_show_action=true">Sep 16, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mali Mor ❤️ The Romantic Blogger" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mali Mor ❤️ The Romantic Blogger" href="/user/show/88472183-mali-mor-the-romantic-blogger">Mali Mor ❤️ The Romantic Blogger</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3551334080" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer968869831514337448"><a href='https://ibb.co/TkRd61b' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1600246445ra/30112973.gif' alt='16-09-2020-11-35-18-2140000' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This is the story of 19-year-old Ashlyn Jennings who lost her best friend and twin sister to leukemia. Her mother sends her to a small town to live with her estranged father and his new family, and on her way their, on the train, she meets a handsome stranger with piercing blue eyes who invites her to see his band play. 💙<br/><br/>They have immediate attraction, but also a deep closeness - because both have a tragic past. After the show they plan to meet again, but before it happens, Ashlyn discovers </span>
  <span id="freeText968869831514337448" style="display:none"><a href="https://ibb.co/TkRd61b" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1600246445ra/30112973.gif" alt="16-09-2020-11-35-18-2140000" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is the story of 19-year-old Ashlyn Jennings who lost her best friend and twin sister to leukemia. Her mother sends her to a small town to live with her estranged father and his new family, and on her way their, on the train, she meets a handsome stranger with piercing blue eyes who invites her to see his band play. 💙<br><br>They have immediate attraction, but also a deep closeness - because both have a tragic past. After the show they plan to meet again, but before it happens, Ashlyn discovers that Daniel Daniels is her new English teacher, Mr. Daniels. (Which is a bit strange, because he's only 22 years old. lol). 💥<br><br>📚 “𝐈 𝐝𝐨𝐧’𝐭 𝐰𝐚𝐧𝐭 𝐭𝐨 𝐛𝐞 𝐲𝐨𝐮𝐫 𝐟𝐫𝐢𝐞𝐧𝐝,” 𝐡𝐞 𝐬𝐚𝐢𝐝. 𝐖𝐞 𝐛𝐫𝐞𝐚𝐭𝐡𝐞𝐝 𝐢𝐧 𝐭𝐨𝐠𝐞𝐭𝐡𝐞𝐫 𝐚𝐧𝐝 𝐞𝐱𝐡𝐚𝐥𝐞𝐝 𝐢𝐧 𝐡𝐚𝐫𝐦𝐨𝐧𝐲. “𝐈 𝐰𝐚𝐧𝐭 𝐭𝐨 𝐛𝐞 𝐲𝐨𝐮𝐫𝐬, 𝐈 𝐰𝐚𝐧𝐭 𝐲𝐨𝐮 𝐭𝐨 𝐛𝐞 𝐦𝐢𝐧𝐞, 𝐚𝐧𝐝 𝐈 𝐡𝐚𝐭𝐞 𝐭𝐡𝐚𝐭 𝐰𝐞 𝐜𝐚𝐧’𝐭 𝐛𝐞 𝐮𝐬. 𝐁𝐞𝐜𝐚𝐮𝐬𝐞 𝐈 𝐭𝐡𝐢𝐧𝐤 𝐰𝐞 𝐰𝐞𝐫𝐞 𝐦𝐞𝐚𝐧𝐭 𝐭𝐨 𝐛𝐞 𝐮𝐬.” 📚<br><br>I enjoyed this book, but two things disappointed me: all the tragedies in the story... and the end, that was too quick (which happens in most of Brittainy's books). <br>It bothered me that Daniel and Ashley's "forbidden" relationship was not the focus of the book, because most of the drama was related to their families...<br>There were too many family tragedies (on both sides) and I did not understand in what way they served the story - but most importantly, some of these issues were not resolved at the end of the book at all...<br>The deaths of family members, drug addiction, alcoholism, bullying, coming out problems... Why the hell did all this happen?? 😱😱😱<br><br>📚 “𝐈 𝐥𝐨𝐯𝐞 𝐲𝐨𝐮 𝐬𝐥𝐨𝐰𝐥𝐲. 𝐈 𝐥𝐨𝐯𝐞 𝐲𝐨𝐮 𝐝𝐞𝐞𝐩𝐥𝐲. 𝐈 𝐥𝐨𝐯𝐞 𝐲𝐨𝐮 𝐪𝐮𝐢𝐞𝐭𝐥𝐲. 𝐈 𝐥𝐨𝐯𝐞 𝐲𝐨𝐮 𝐩𝐨𝐰𝐞𝐫𝐟𝐮𝐥𝐥𝐲. 𝐈 𝐥𝐨𝐯𝐞 𝐲𝐨𝐮 𝐮𝐧𝐜𝐨𝐧𝐝𝐢𝐭𝐢𝐨𝐧𝐚𝐥𝐥𝐲.” 📚<br><br>However, Daniel was an amazing character who managed to get into my heart.<br>It's a book about loss and pain... about coping and forgiveness... and of course, LOVE. A sweet romance (which didn’t really feel forbidden to me) about 2 people who fell in love with the right people, at the wrong time. 💙💙💙<br><br>• I listened to the AUDIO version. 🎧 <br><br>▪️▫️▪️▫️▪️▫️▪️▫️▪️▫️▪️▫️▪️▫️▪️▫️<br><br>📖 ᖴOᒪᒪOᗯ ᗰE Oᑎ IᑎᔕTᗩGᖇᗩᗰ: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.instagram.com/the_romantic_blogger/">https://www.instagram.com/the_romanti...</a><br><br>📖 ᐯIᔕIT ᗰY ᗷᒪOG ᖴOᖇ ᗰOᖇE ᖇEᐯIEᗯᔕ: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://books-romance.com/">https://books-romance.com/</a><br><br>📖 GOOᗪᖇEᗩᗪᔕ: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://bit.ly/3acMRMP">https://bit.ly/3acMRMP</a><br><br>💕 לקריאת הסקירה בעברית, כנסו לבלוג: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://books-romance.com/">https://books-romance.com/</a> 💕</span>

  <span id="freeText3847220142124449179" style="display:none">5++++++++ stars!!!! HOLY EPIC AMAZINGNESS!!!<br><br>“Always remember our first glance,<br>And I’ll promise your heart that I’ll be enough.”<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400020755i/9623682.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>“His eyes were so blue and filled with interest. <span id="freeTextContainer7375350096480322234">I thought this would be a romance between a student and a teacher. What I read was a story about human nature and life’s poetic moments. Real life expressed through every spectrum. I laughed and cried through every page of this book. I was meant to beta read it and give Brittainy feedback. I couldn’t give her a single thing. <br/><br/>I’m sure you’ve heard the idea that everyone has a story living inside of them. <br/><br/>Throughout reading this book, I couldn’t help but feel like this was Brittainy’s story— Her s</span>
  <span id="freeText7375350096480322234" style="display:none">I thought this would be a romance between a student and a teacher. What I read was a story about human nature and life’s poetic moments. Real life expressed through every spectrum. I laughed and cried through every page of this book. I was meant to beta read it and give Brittainy feedback. I couldn’t give her a single thing. <br><br>I’m sure you’ve heard the idea that everyone has a story living inside of them. <br><br>Throughout reading this book, I couldn’t help but feel like this was Brittainy’s story— Her story told with such aching beauty that I had to highlight something on every page just to remind myself of her beautiful words.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=28lqbcx" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396562405i/9152985.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This story was about Family. Secrets. Appearances. Grief. Laughter. Shakespeare. Love. Each character had their own journey and I felt connected to each and every one of them. Ryan was my favorite, but he won’t be everyone’s favorite, because that’s the beauty of this story. I think each reader will connect with it in a fresh and genuine way so that we’re each left with a unique and wholly personal experience.<br><br>This is a story for someone that wants <i>more</i>. Something deeper that will stick with them even after the story ends.<br><br>I’m so proud of Brittainy. This is her story. <b>Her Golden.</b><br></span>

<div id="review_933296517" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/933296517" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/933296517?book_show_action=true">May 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Brittainy C. Cherry Fan, New Age Fans, Everyone</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Wendy'sThoughts by: </span>
      Patrycja
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer933296517" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10157992737888417639"><b>5 Coping with Real Life<br/>* * * * * <i>Spoiler Free</i><br/>This is an experience... overwhelming, intense and so heartfelt. There are moments that will make you stop and just absorb it all... because of the quirky beauty and then the deep, slicing pain. If I sound a little overly dramatic with this book, it's because I never was a bystander. What do I mean by that? It's when you are reading and kinda going through the motions; you are there ... and then you drift away... maybe go and fix a little snack... tal</b></span>
  <span id="freeText10157992737888417639" style="display:none"><b>5 Coping with Real Life<br>* * * * * <i>Spoiler Free</i><br>This is an experience... overwhelming, intense and so heartfelt. There are moments that will make you stop and just absorb it all... because of the quirky beauty and then the deep, slicing pain. If I sound a little overly dramatic with this book, it's because I never was a bystander. What do I mean by that? It's when you are reading and kinda going through the motions; you are there ... and then you drift away... maybe go and fix a little snack... talk on the phone with a friend or check your email. You're not fully invested. This read demands you tuck in and give yourself over to it from the start. If you don't, it will be your loss.<br><br>There is so much covered in this book; the use of a teacher and the older student is the least of the things it's about in my opinion. It focuses on sibling and parental loss; the undercurrent of blame and how it can be destructive in so many ways. Bullying, sexual orientation, and acceptance are also addressed. </b><br><br>But mostly right next to all of these deep issues which cause unbearable pain for those in it...this story gives us pure and staggering love... first love and sibling love ... <br><br>The rush we feel with this first love and way it is nourished and blossoms is beyond any description I can give you...it will wash over you as you read how it happens; tentative steps all done against the artistry of Shakespeare. This first love is also teamed with the love of sisters with a special bond only twins can have.<br><br>So, this tale is chocked full of thought proving ideas... and it kills me not to go into all of them... but then I would be telling you this story instead of you experiencing it as I did... which was primarily going into it blind. I will share all of the characters were so well crafted... there are no missing pieces with them... they held their own, I was there with their crisis' too.<br><br>This period in life...is so hard... and there is a scene which addresses it so eloquently... I don't think it could be done better.<br><br>Brittainy C. Cherry wrote something very special and I am better for reading it. Patrycja's review pushed me over the edge in reading this today and I am most appreciative. If you are looking for something which will cause you to think about life and how you live it... then don't be a bystander... read this book. <br><br><i>Book provided to our blog by the Author in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br><strong>For more Reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong><br><div>
  <br>
  <a href="http://starangelsreviews.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img alt=" photo banner_zpsb3ab83a0.jpg" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407612151i/10746470._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2374049172" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12546986370024874280"><b> 4.5 stars! </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “Leave the past behind you so the future can find you.” </i> </b><br/><br/>Once upon a time.... a friend recommended this book to me. Well, four years later and I finally read it!!!!!!! See, I eventually get to books on my TBR!<br/><br/>Loving Mr. Daniels is about two broken people who have lost family members closest to them. When Ashlynn moves in with her dad, the last thing she expected was to fall for a Shakespearean inspired musician. And she's even more surprised when he turns out to be her teacher.<br/><br/>I kn</span>
  <span id="freeText12546986370024874280" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 stars! </b><br><br><b> <i> “Leave the past behind you so the future can find you.” </i> </b><br><br>Once upon a time.... a friend recommended this book to me. Well, four years later and I finally read it!!!!!!! See, I eventually get to books on my TBR!<br><br>Loving Mr. Daniels is about two broken people who have lost family members closest to them. When Ashlynn moves in with her dad, the last thing she expected was to fall for a Shakespearean inspired musician. And she's even more surprised when he turns out to be her teacher.<br><br>I know what you're thinking, that you've read this book already. Yes, you've read this trope, but Cherry puts her own beautiful spin on it and I loved this book. Bravo Ms Cherry! I do wish she wasn't so good at making me cry, but I think that's a testament to her writing skills.<br><br>I hope you all give this book a chance! I did, years later and I loved it! It's never too late!<br><br><b> <i> “I love you slowly. I love you deeply. I love you quietly. I love you powerfully. I love you unconditionally.” </i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494101706i/22685352._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Follow me on ♥ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> ♥ <a href="http://rachelsreadsravenously.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> ♥ <a href="http://instagram.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ♥ <a href="https://twitter.com/rayliz89" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> ♥</span>

<div id="review_902398985" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/902398985" />
    <a title="Maayan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13323856-maayan"><img alt="Maayan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576662192p2/13323856.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/902398985?book_show_action=true">Apr 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maayan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maayan" href="/user/show/13323856-maayan">Maayan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13323856-maayan?shelf=teacher-student">teacher-student</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13323856-maayan?shelf=my-favorite-books">my-favorite-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13323856-maayan?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13323856-maayan?shelf=safety-gang-safe">safety-gang-safe</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13323856-maayan?shelf=musicians">musicians</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13323856-maayan?shelf=older-man-younger-woman">older-man-younger-woman</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13323856-maayan?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13323856-maayan?shelf=hero-pushing-away">hero-pushing-away</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer902398985" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10655689886073126703"><b><i>♫"Always remember our first glance,<br/>And I'll promise your heart that I'll be enough."♫</i><br/>-Romeo's Quest.</b><br/><br/>Usually when I'm starting a Teacher/Student book I know <b>exactly</b> what I'm getting myself into. The <b>plot</b> is always the same. The <b>angst</b> is always the same. The <b>problems the couple is faced</b> are <b>usually</b> the same. When I started the book <b>
  <i>'Loving Mr. Daniels'</i>
</b> I was sure I'm gonna read the average forbidden love story. What I got <b>Blew me away.</b> <br/><br/><b>
  <i>"The best things in life aren't easy. They are tough, t</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText10655689886073126703" style="display:none"><b><i>♫"Always remember our first glance,<br>And I'll promise your heart that I'll be enough."♫</i><br>-Romeo's Quest.</b><br><br>Usually when I'm starting a Teacher/Student book I know <b>exactly</b> what I'm getting myself into. The <b>plot</b> is always the same. The <b>angst</b> is always the same. The <b>problems the couple is faced</b> are <b>usually</b> the same. When I started the book <b>
  <i>'Loving Mr. Daniels'</i>
</b> I was sure I'm gonna read the average forbidden love story. What I got <b>Blew me away.</b> <br><br><b>
  <i>"The best things in life aren't easy. They are tough, they are painful, and they are raw. That makes the arrival to the final destination that much sweeter."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398431141i/9412330._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When we meet Daniel&amp;Ashlyn, both went through some kind of tragedy in their life. They are <b>lost.</b> They are <b>lonely.</b> They are <b>sad.</b> They are <b>broken.</b> They go with the motion of life, but they don't <b>LIVE.</b> When they meet each other, something inside of them start to stir. They are starting to <b>wake up</b> after been asleep for so long. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399804511i/9597859._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"There had been one moment when i saw someone who might understand, based solely on her eyes. Her eyes were surreal, haunting even. Green, powerful eyes that looked so sad. Broken. Beautiful."</b><br><br>When they first meet at the train station, both didn't know it's going to be the start of something, <br>overwhelming<br>Fulfilling<br>beautiful <br>exciting<br>Amazing<br><b>Forbidden.</b><br><br>After seeing her that first time, and his inability of letting her go without an excuse to see her again, Daniel invite Ashlyn to see his band 'Romeo's Quest' show. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398276227i/9394518._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"He gripped the microphone in the stand in his large hands and cradled it like it was his lover, and when his eyes looked up into the audience, he found my stare. He nodded once at me, and as he finished the final words of the song, I felt he were giving me a privet concert."</b><br><br>Their interaction, their banter, their playfulness .. It was so fun to read. Their connection felt so REAL. Like they knew each other for the longest time. They spend a magical night together, where they let go of the restraints holding them back and finally, let go of all the Demons deep inside, and set each other free. At least, for a night &lt;3<br><br><b>"He moved his mouth away from mine, leaving me with my eyes closed and my heart open. I could feel his heart pounding against his t-shirt, and he placed his hand over my heart. Words were not needed because everything was felt from within, spilling out into each other's fingertips."</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394029581ra/8798112.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As a result of being sick in the past, Ashlyn was held back a year. Now she's 19 years old at her last year of high school. New town. New place. New people. <b>New love.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398276227i/9394519._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When she gets to her last lesson of the day, first day of school, she can't believe her eyes. Daniel. Her Daniel is Mr. Daniels - her 22 years old new English teacher. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398276227i/9394520.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I miss you so much it's hard to breathe."</i>
</b><br><br>After the discovery of the obstacle standing in the way of their love, both were facing the new reality. They wanted each other, Wanted to be together, but at the same time, can't let themselves hurt each other in the long run. Daniel started to think about <b>breaking the rules, finding the loopholes</b>, and Ashlyn felt that something important inside of her is <b>missing.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398276227ra/9394521.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"I just wish i didn't like you so much." I didn't know why, but i felt like crying when he said that. Beacuse i liked him too. I closed my eyes and allowed his scents to wash over me, bathing me in fantasy and false hope. When my eyes reopend, I saw his stare, strong and determined. He took my arm and pulled me around to a corner and we went through a door to an empty staircase. He glanced up and down the stairs before he pressed his mouth against mine."</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398276227ra/9394522.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I hated how my other students looked at her. How they lusted after her. I hated how much i missed her lips, her laugh. Her smile. I hated how close she was but how distant we felt. I loved how beautiful she looked each and every day. I loved how, when i went on runs, she joined me in the front of my mind. I loved how she was effortlessly beautiful. I loved how she moved. How she stood. How she sat. I loved how distant we were but how close we felt."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398276227ra/9394523.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Besides her doomed love life, Ashlyn needed to face bullies, repair her relationship with her dad, grieve on her sister, forgive her mother, worry about her new allies, continue with her writing, and find some balance in her new life.<br><br>What I loved the most in the book was even thought both of them couldn't be with each other Physically they were with each other mentally.<b>They never stopped wanting. Needing. Yearning.</b> They didn't look for other people to fill the void. They were completely devoted to each other through ALL THE BOOK! <br><br><b>"His lips turned up in a half smirk and my lips followed, giving him the other half. We made each other smile without even saying a word."</b><br><br>When both couldn't deny their feelings anymore, and drawn back into each others arms, they started an EPIC and forbidden love story. It was so natural, so easy. Their relationship never felt forced and i LOVED this in the book. <br><br><b>"Why did you have to be my student?"<br>A smile crept on my face. "Beacuse God has a sick sense of humor."</b><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398276427i/9394536.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"I love you slowly," I said, "I love you deeply." My mouth moved to her earlobe, and i whispered as i sucked it slowly, "I love you quietly." My hips rolled against her, my breaths heavy, hungry. "I love you powerfully." Her head fell against the wall, her breaths mere pants. "I love you unconditionally. I love you gently and hard, slow and fast. Before time and after. I love you Beacuse i was born to do so." Before her, i never knew life. After her, I'd never know death."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387814432i/7674934._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"My bounty is as boundless as the sea. My love is as deep; The more i give to tee. The more i have, for both are infinite."</i>
</b><br><br>I just loved the whole Shakespeare Theme ! I think the author Combined The quotes and the references beautifully! Both shared a Unique love for Shakespeare. It was a huge connecting subject for them.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398276227i/9394526.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"When we are born, we cry that we are to come to this great stage of fools."</i>
</b><br><br>The things they were dealing with were so REAL! Both has fears, both Struggled keeping their love a secret and not shouting it to the world. Both felt the yearning to touch and comfort each other in public. Both needed to adjust to this forbidden relationship. When outside forces trying to come between them (don't worry! It's not a woman/man after the heroes. Anything like that) what will they do to keep each other safe ?<br><br><b>"This is home, Ashlyn. We are home."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399804511i/9597860._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved the secondary characters so much!! Every one of them had their own story to tell. Had their own journey to face. Had their own voice to yell. They were so alive! I felt their emotions and each one of them added to the story. I can say with my whole heart that Ryan was my favorite. I loved this guy. He was a magnetic force pulling Everyone to him.<br><br>Now .. let's talk about the 80% mark. Gosh. It <b>Killed</b> me. It <b>Destroyed</b> me. It <b>wracked</b> me. I seriously didn't saw it coming. It breaks my heart just remembering it. DON'T read spoilers. When you get to the scene you need to to feel it without previous knowledge. It will make it so much powerful. Trust me on it. I sobbed for a few minutes, trying to calm myself down. Why oh why did you do it ?!?!? So sad ..<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391889308ra/8471651.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When life get in the way of our couple, they had to make a few important decisions about the future. How their love story will end? Is love conquers all?<br><br>This you'll have to find out yourself ;)<br><br><b>"No such thing as a second chance, Only first chances that never end."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398276227i/9394527._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“ARC provided by author in exchange for an honest review”</i>
</b><br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2005500543?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Effy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Effy" href="/user/show/26874718-effy">Effy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26874718-effy?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26874718-effy?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26874718-effy?shelf=forbidden-romance">forbidden-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26874718-effy?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2005500543" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6673096449787386645"><blockquote>“Because pretending to be happy is almost like being happy. Until you remember that you’re only pretending. Then you’re sad. Really sad. Because wearing a mask every day of your life is the hardest thing to do. And after a while, you get a little scared because the mask becomes you.”</blockquote><br/><p><i>'Student-teacher romances'</i> are not right up my alley. Unsurprisingly, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20348781.Loving_Mr__Daniels' title='Loving Mr. Daniels by Brittainy C. Cherry' rel='nofollow noopener'>Loving Mr. Daniels</a> was not my cup of tea.</p><br/><p>The novel follows Ashlyn, a senior, grief-stricken student who is mourning her twin sister, Gabby, who ha</p></span>
  <span id="freeText6673096449787386645" style="display:none"><blockquote>“Because pretending to be happy is almost like being happy. Until you remember that you’re only pretending. Then you’re sad. Really sad. Because wearing a mask every day of your life is the hardest thing to do. And after a while, you get a little scared because the mask becomes you.”</blockquote><br /><p><i>'Student-teacher romances'</i> are not right up my alley. Unsurprisingly, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20348781.Loving_Mr__Daniels" title="Loving Mr. Daniels by Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">Loving Mr. Daniels</a> was not my cup of tea.</p><br /><p>The novel follows Ashlyn, a senior, grief-stricken student who is mourning her twin sister, Gabby, who has recently passed away. She stumbles across a handsome stranger on the train on her way to the city she's moving to and has an instant connection with him. Being completely swept off her feet, she faces an insurmountable obstacle when he turns out to be her school teacher.</p><br /><p>The <i>story</i> was <i>cheesy</i> and <i>corny</i> and I would even go as far as to describe it as <i>overdramatic</i>. The protagonists' <i>attraction</i> was <i>'insta-lovey'</i> and I was not emotionally attached to them at all. They were <i>one-dimensional</i> and I could not care less about them. The <i>story</i> was <i>dull</i> and <i>boring</i> and I felt like nothing was happening for the most part of the book.</p><br /><p><u>Things I appreciated about the book:</u> <i>the powerful relationship between Ashlyn and Gabby, the bucket list Gabby made on account of Ashlyn and the letters she had directed her sister to read once she had crossed off an item she had completed, the references to Shakespeare, Daniel's band that was named 'Romeo's Quest' and the lyrics at the beginning of each chapter.</i></p><br /><p>I cannot pinpoint exactly the reason for my being mildly <i>apathetic</i> about the story. The shadow of <i>death, loss</i> and <i>grief</i> was superabundant. I may have to come to terms with the fact that nothing <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7121791.Brittainy_C__Cherry" title="Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">Brittainy C. Cherry</a> has come up with can beat <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/32294951.The_Gravity_of_Us__Elements___4_" title="The Gravity of Us (Elements, #4) by Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">The Gravity of Us</a>.</p></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1403625339?book_show_action=true">Sep 05, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hulya Kara Yuksel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hulya Kara Yuksel" href="/user/show/32793174-hulya-kara-yuksel">Hulya Kara Yuksel</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22071325-loving-mr-daniels">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1403625339" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11286924829978830900"><i> <b>“I love you slowly. I love you deeply. I love you quietly. I love you powerfully.   <span id="freeText11286924829978830900" style="display:none"><i> <b>“I love you slowly. I love you deeply. I love you quietly. I love you powerfully.         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1218513344" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16379554466029254513"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430137013i/14685052._SY540_.jpg' width='275' height='275' alt='Loving Mr Daniels' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><i>
  <b>"Maybe there weren't two different Daniels. Maybe Mr. Daniels was just another part of him. So it wasn't surprising that I had fallen for both sides of the coin. I was crazy about all of him-- the good, the bad, and the broken pieces."</b>
</i> <br/><br/>Every time I finish a book that is so beautiful and phenomenal, I always find it hard to make a review. It's as if words are not enough to describe how great it is. <br/><br/>So, can I just say first and foremost that <b>THIS BOOK IS REALLY AMAZING?</b> Honesty, if there's a </span>
  <span id="freeText16379554466029254513" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430137013i/14685052._SY540_.jpg" width="275" height="275" alt="Loving Mr Daniels" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>
  <b>"Maybe there weren't two different Daniels. Maybe Mr. Daniels was just another part of him. So it wasn't surprising that I had fallen for both sides of the coin. I was crazy about all of him-- the good, the bad, and the broken pieces."</b>
</i> <br><br>Every time I finish a book that is so beautiful and phenomenal, I always find it hard to make a review. It's as if words are not enough to describe how great it is. <br><br>So, can I just say first and foremost that <b>THIS BOOK IS REALLY AMAZING?</b> Honesty, if there's a word greater than 'amazing', then that's how I describe this book. <b>I LOVE IT WAY TOO MUCH</b> that it breaks my heart!<br><br>From the start to the middle part until the very end, I never had a dull moment reading it because the characters are so likeable and they already created a special space in my heart. The plot is beautiful and heartwarming, and so is the setting and the whole concept. This book is uniquely told, poignant, and totally sweet in every way.<br><br>There are so many things I have learned from this book. Not only does it tell about a story of two persons who found love in each other through their similarities and painful situations but it also depicts family drama that will tug your heart.<br><br><b>I DID CRY.</b> In a good way. Even if I've already expected it, I found myself really affected because the scenes in this book are just totally compelling. It's like watching a Nicholas Sparks flick, you know. You just can't control your emotions. More importantly, I found myself really in love while reading it. It's a nice feeling. ;) <br><br>I see that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7121791.Brittainy_C__Cherry" title="Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">Brittainy C. Cherry</a> is not that really well-known as an author, unlike other contemporary authors but I think she deserves the highlight, guys. She's awesome! She's a very talented author and this book proves it right. I like her writing style. The way she creates those quotable lines-- I could highlight the whole book! Totally amazing! This book, for sure, will never be the last book that I will read from this author.<br><br>As a whole, this book is spectacular. You guys should definitely check this out because if you haven't read this book yet, you sure are missing half of your life! :)<br><br>Rating: 5 Stars<br><br>Book review also posted on my blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://bibliopearl.wordpress.com/2015/04/27/review-loving-mr-daniels-by-brittainy-c-cherry/">https://bibliopearl.wordpress.com/201...</a><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2503143349958578575"><b>4.5 ~ 5 GOLDEN Stars</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>”I want to be yours, I want you to me mine, and I hate that we can’t be us. Because I think we are meant to be us.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>Where to begin, this story was so damn good! Tears will be shed while you take this heartbreakingly beautiful journey. The story is told in alternating pov, there is a ton of Shakespeare quoted and manipulated while our two main characters build a relationship that so many people only dream of. <br/><br/>Ashlyn’s twin sister Gabby passes away and her mothe</span>
  <span id="freeText2503143349958578575" style="display:none"><b>4.5 ~ 5 GOLDEN Stars</b><br><br><b>
  <i>”I want to be yours, I want you to me mine, and I hate that we can’t be us. Because I think we are meant to be us.”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Where to begin, this story was so damn good! Tears will be shed while you take this heartbreakingly beautiful journey. The story is told in alternating pov, there is a ton of Shakespeare quoted and manipulated while our two main characters build a relationship that so many people only dream of. <br><br>Ashlyn’s twin sister Gabby passes away and her mother is struggling so she is sent to attend her senior year in her father’s school where he is the principal. Her father has been pretty absente during Ashlyn’s life and when she arrives she finds that he has a full family in place. Ryan and Hailey were fantastic as was all the secondary characters in this story.<br><br>On a train ride to her father’s home in Wisconsin, she meets Daniel Daniels and the attraction and connection is magic! They spend time together and then BAAM the two find out they are teacher/student for the year. <br><br><b>
  <i>”You don’t deserve to be someone’s secret, Ashlyn. You deserve to be the chorus to a person’s favorite song.”</i>
</b><br><br>In true teacher/student they try to stay away, they try sneaking around and all along Ashlyn grows and heals while their bond just gets stronger.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>While the love between Daniel and Ashlyn’s soars even when they are apart, Ashlyn’s relationship with Ryan and Hailey grows as well. She tries to help them in their lives and finds a family with them.<br><br>I must note that her sister Gabby has put together a bucket list accompanied by letters to open when she completes each task. In this manner, the author brilliantly makes Gabby an important part of the story to the very end.<br><br>My one issue was that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ if things had panned out for my favorite character, I would have been reading my first m/m book because I loved him to pieces and would have read anything that he was in. I sincerely believe this was a <b>POOR</b> move on the author’s part because fans would have happily one clicked for his book.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492029733ra/22475256.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Other than my “issue” I still give this book 5 Stars and strongly believe it’s worth every tear and am I'm still choked up while wearing a big smile!<br><br><b>
  <i>"Make me your golden."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492029733ra/22475258.gif" width="390" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_932636443" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/932636443" />
    <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27276528-liz"><img alt="✰ Liz ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451097545p2/27276528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/932636443?book_show_action=true">May 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=best-couples">best-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=healing">healing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=high-angst-alert">high-angst-alert</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=must-read">must-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer932636443" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5709199111515454146"><b>"I was convinced that everyone in the world had a form of weirdness to them. And the cool thing, at least I hoped so, was the idea that there was someone out there just as quirky as you were. The idea of finding your other weirdo was so attractive to me." </b><br/><br/>Brittainy C. Cherry is a goddess of text and heart. Loving Mr. Daniels was a beautiful read that has stayed with me days after. I was so hesitant to read this book. First of all, being a teacher, I am just not comfortable with the teacher stude</span>
  <span id="freeText5709199111515454146" style="display:none"><b>"I was convinced that everyone in the world had a form of weirdness to them. And the cool thing, at least I hoped so, was the idea that there was someone out there just as quirky as you were. The idea of finding your other weirdo was so attractive to me." </b><br><br>Brittainy C. Cherry is a goddess of text and heart. Loving Mr. Daniels was a beautiful read that has stayed with me days after. I was so hesitant to read this book. First of all, being a teacher, I am just not comfortable with the teacher student romances. Secondly, lately it seems I have been avoiding books with any hint of angst like the plague. However, I decided to take the plunge....how bad could it be? Let me just say to those of you that are waiting to read this, don't wait another second. Crack it open and read it. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418588533i/12842294._SX540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Ashlyn is a beautiful young adult. Because of having an illness as a young child, she was held back in school. This makes her an 19 year old senior. As the book begins, she is experiencing a terrible loss. As if things could not be worse for her, her mother is sending her away. Ashlyn is forced to move away her senior year and live with a father that she doesn't know. Ashlyn is feeling so lost and alone. She is missing her sister and trying to find her way through each moment.<br><br> <b>"People always said it would get easier after losing someone. People said that, over time, it would get better. But I couldn’t comprehend how that could be true. As each day passed, it just became harder. The world only grew darker. The pain merely deepened."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418588533i/12842295.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As Ashlyn makes her way to her new home, she meets a man that will change her life. <br><br> <b>"Beautiful. Breathtaking. Brilliant. Blue eyes." </b><br><br>Right from the instant they meet they realize they both love Shakespeare, This man, like her sister, is a musician. His name is Daniel. He invites her to a club to hear him play. Meeting Daniel is like a piece of strength pressing down on her broken heart.<br><br><b>“Bye,” I whispered, watching the car pull off. I didn’t look away until it rounded the corner out of the lot and went far, far away. I looked down to my book clenched in my hands and smiled. I was going to start from the beginning again.</b><br><br>When Ashlyn arrives at her new home, she discovers that her father has a new family. She feels like an outsider. The dynamics of living with a man who has never been your father and watching him be a father to someone else causes Ashlyn to recognize just how lost she truly is.<br><br><b>"The awkwardness of the situation set in and I came to a strong resolution. I knew nothing about Henry and this family seemed to know everything. I knew it was stupid, but a part of me was pretty saddened by that. Why was it that you wanted those who ignored you to love you the most?"</b><br><br>Unwanted and broken, she makes her way to the club to her Daniel play.<br><br>Daniel is no secret to heartbreak and pain. Seeing Ashlyn break down before she even makes it inside the club. He calms her. He soothes her. He recognizes that she is significant to him. Ashlyn and Daniel make sense. After their first kiss, their fate is sealed. As the saying goes, what is meant to be well be.<br><br> <b>"The overwhelming amount of emotions running through my body electrified the energy that traveled from me to him. I knew I would never want to kiss another man from the way I kissed him. I never knew that kissing could be so simple yet so complex. He did all of the work with just his lips discovering mine."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418588533i/12842296.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>As Ashlyn grows closer to her "new" brother and sister, she continues to text Daniel. Their friendship blossoms and she finds piece in knowing there is someone out there who can give her joy. She is still trying to find her place with her father. As she makes her way to her first day of her senior year, she faces bullies, pressure, and the worst possible scenario is put in to place. (Can this poor girl please just catch a break?) Her AP English teacher is Daniel. HER DANIEL! Just as she drops her schedule in a fit, he picks it up.<br><br><b>"He studied it, his eyes growing more and more worried. “You’re a student.” His hand formed a fist and he repeatedly tapped it against his mouth. “You’re my student.”</b><br><br>And now, the rest of the story. Daniel and Ashlyn have to face the facts that they are in love. Even though she is 19, Daniel is her teacher. Her father is the assistant principal. Things just couldn't be worse. Or is it that things could not be better? Can we really control who we fall in love with?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410629852i/11133510.jpg" width="350" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>“You’re the reason people believe in tomorrow. You’re the voice that scares the shadows away. You’re the love that makes me breathe. So for the next few seconds, I’m going to be selfish. I’m going to say things that I don’t want you to listen to. Stay with me forever. Please, Ashlyn. Let me be your everything. Make me your golden." </b><br><br>This book has everything. Heart, passion, love, loss, friendship, and everything in between. I was never bored. The tension between the characters and the obstacles they face are enough to keep you engaged but not so much that you can't handle it! I would recommend this book to absolutely anyone. I am sure that in a few months I will pick it up and read it again. There is something magical about falling in love and finding your someone. Don't wait...read this beauty now! Your heart will be flooded with love! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418588533i/12842297._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>"Home. That’s what we were… We were home."</b><br><br><b>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:</b><br><br><a href="https://craziesrusbookblog.wordpress.com//" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434387282i/15214674._SX540_.jpg" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450764696i/17467413.jpg" width="" height="50" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><a href="https://twitter.com/CraziesRus" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450633462i/17450183.png" width="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1043141246" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1043141246" />
    <a title="NMmomof4" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4"><img alt="NMmomof4" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515474309p2/24665574.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1043141246?book_show_action=true">Sep 02, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NMmomof4" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NMmomof4" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4">NMmomof4</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=tears">tears</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=safe">safe</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=hs">hs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=musician">musician</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=separation-without-other-partners">separation-without-other-partners</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=kindle-unlimited">kindle-unlimited</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=workplace">workplace</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=taboo">taboo</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1043141246" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7096907366127956284"><b> 5 Stars <i> (Originally Read - 9/2/2014)</i></b><br/><br/><b> 5 Stars <i> (Re-Read - 8/22/2018)</i></b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b>Wow. This was still an emotional read! I wasn't expecting to go through all the feelings I did the second go-round. I honestly put off doing this re-read because I was afraid it'd be like some other books that I deemed my "favorites" where it didn't hold up the second time, but I'm glad to report this is keeping its 5 star rating and staying firmly on my favorites shelf! I know I get in the mood for an emotiona</span>
  <span id="freeText7096907366127956284" style="display:none"><b> 5 Stars <i> (Originally Read - 9/2/2014)</i></b><br /><br /><b> 5 Stars <i> (Re-Read - 8/22/2018)</i></b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b>Wow. This was still an emotional read! I wasn't expecting to go through all the feelings I did the second go-round. I honestly put off doing this re-read because I was afraid it'd be like some other books that I deemed my "favorites" where it didn't hold up the second time, but I'm glad to report this is keeping its 5 star rating and staying firmly on my favorites shelf! I know I get in the mood for an emotional of book sometimes -- so, I highly recommend it if you're looking for a good cry! I really did love their relationship too. The Shakespeare's stuff was a tad cheesy at times, but I thought it worked for them. I truly felt like they were meant to be, and I think that allowed me to be alright with the ending even though I would've loved more! Great book.<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Ashlynn and Daniel's story. Ashlynn just lost her twin sister to cancer, and her mom sends her off to her estranged father for her senior year of high school because she is having trouble coping. She meets this guy in the train into town and they hit it off instantly, and she ends up going to his band's performance at a local bar a few days later. They connect through their grief of losing love ones and Shakespeare. They are both shocked to find out that Ashlynn is in Daniel's senior AP language arts class. They struggle a lot with their new reality, but they cannot deny the intense feelings they still feel for one another. There is some family and friend drama, some heartbreaking moments, and a few sexy times...and they get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between Ashlynn and Daniel's POV.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. I never skimmed and I thought it flowed well.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No, they take a while to express stronger feelings. They do feel an instant intense connection though.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Daniel. I liked him. I appreciated how he always tried to do the right thing even when it was tough (like with his brother). I also liked how he understood and supported Ashlynn through her grief.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 3.5 stars. Ashlynn. I liked her. I did struggle with her at times though. I wanted to shake her about her dad as well as her constant crying (I'm sorry if that makes me a bad person, because I totally get that she had a LOT of punches to roll with, but it got kinda old for me).<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Moderate/high. I cried a good bit for the last 1/3 of the book even this time reading it. The first time I read it, I remember feeling wrecked!<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Both the h and H have times where they push away and also pursue the relationship.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Low. They have okay tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not very many descriptive scenes and not so much it takes away from the story. I would say that they are more about the emotional connection rather than the physical.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Kind of. Not quite fade-to-black for most scenes but close. Some scenes are more descriptive.<br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ There is a OM at the h's school that is interested and strongly pursues her, and this causes jealousy for the H. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> No<br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are separated a few times with the longest being ~3 years, but there was no mention or suggestion of other partners during this time.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Loss of loved ones (off and on page), drug use/abuse/drug addiction/alcoholism (side characters), taboo teacher/student relationship (on page), the H is ~3 years older than the h (19/22), and suicide of a side character (aftermath on page) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had pretty good closure with what I would call a HEA ending. Would I have liked a farther glimpse into their future? Of course. That's my greedy self speaking for sure 😜<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one should be <u>Safe</u> for most safety gang readers<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have both the h and H pushing away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a few separations between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1251918950" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3828085572951599859"><i>first read: April 12, 2015<br/>first reread: June 20, 2015<br/>second reread: April 6-9, 2016<br/>third reread: March 28 - ?, 2017</i><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>“If I learned anything these past few months, it's that life sucks, Daniel. It sucks. It's mean, it's vicious, and it's unapologetic. It's dark and cruel. But then, sometimes, it's so beautiful that it knocks all of that darkness out of your system with the light.”</i>
</blockquote><br/><b>JUNE 2015:</b> <i>MAYBE, just maybe...after rereading <i>this</i> 2015 Favorite I will stop rereading 2015 favorites and read new </i></span>
  <span id="freeText3828085572951599859" style="display:none"><i>first read: April 12, 2015<br />first reread: June 20, 2015<br />second reread: April 6-9, 2016<br />third reread: March 28 - ?, 2017</i><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“If I learned anything these past few months, it's that life sucks, Daniel. It sucks. It's mean, it's vicious, and it's unapologetic. It's dark and cruel. But then, sometimes, it's so beautiful that it knocks all of that darkness out of your system with the light.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><b>JUNE 2015:</b> <i>MAYBE, just maybe...after rereading <i>this</i> 2015 Favorite I will stop rereading 2015 favorites and read new books....</i><br /><br />I don't think there will ever be a time that I can read this without crying my damn eyes out. The first review from April definitely still stands! I love this story, its just as <i>devastatingly beautiful</i> the 2nd time around, and I have a feeling it'll be like that when it comes to reading it for the 5th, 20th, and 50th time.<br /><br />--------<br /><br /><b>APRIL 2015:</b> <s>I need a minute to calm myself down.............<i>breathe, Ashley....you're good. This book.......wow......I can't even..........where do I start........breeaaaaaaaathe..........</i><br /><br />OKAY, so.....this book....my God, this book....<b>BEAUTIFUL, SO AMAZINGLY, AND EMOTIONALLY, AND DEVASTATINGLY BEAUTIFUL</b>. <br /><br />It is 5 am, I haven't slept...I started this one really late, thinking it was going to be some lighthearted, silly, easy read.....but I was so, so, so wrong....This book had me tearing up from the very beginning, and the tears never went away. This is some real shit, seriously. <b>do not</b> mistake this for some lighthearted entertainment, <b>this is not even close.</b><br /><br />The characters are amazing. I LOVED Daniel, and I LOVED Ashlyn. Both suffering losses, but they find hope and love and a future in each other....I loved every minute of this. <i>And Daniels band?? Heck yes, all the lyrics at the beginning of the chapters, I want this band to be real-life, seriously.</i> The family drama is real, the problems are real....its not like other books where someone mentions something awful happening, you are right there experiencing it and feeling the pain. <br /><br />I loved laughing with Ashlyn, and crying with Ashlyn, and smiling with Ashlyn, and loving with Ashlyn. I loved this book so much, and I would definitely, definitely [if you read the book you'd see what I just did there ;)] recommend it.</s><br /><br /><i>come find me:<br /><b>IG:</b> ash.reads</i></span>

<div id="review_1036616512" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1036616512" />
    <a title="Rag" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25192009-rag"><img alt="Rag" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1562619931p2/25192009.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1036616512?book_show_action=true">Aug 25, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rag" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rag" href="/user/show/25192009-rag">Rag</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25192009-rag?shelf=book-boyfriend">book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25192009-rag?shelf=high-school">high-school</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25192009-rag?shelf=musicians">musicians</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25192009-rag?shelf=teacher-student-romance">teacher-student-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1036616512" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6846430099597649859"><b>5 'Golden' Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpsrb3ic2g6.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445779786i/16702241._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo image_zpsrb3ic2g6.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This book is about Ashlyn and Daniel. Both characters know what it's like to lose an important someone in their lives. They also know what loneliness is like. <br/><br/><b>I was almost certain that loneliness was a disease. An infectious, disgusting illness that was slow to creep into your system and overtake you, even though you tried to fight it off the best you could</b><br/><br/>After Ashlyn's twin, Gabby, died Ashlyn's mom made her go live with her father and his family. Her father was never there</span>
  <span id="freeText6846430099597649859" style="display:none"><b>5 'Golden' Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpsrb3ic2g6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445779786i/16702241._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsrb3ic2g6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This book is about Ashlyn and Daniel. Both characters know what it's like to lose an important someone in their lives. They also know what loneliness is like. <br><br><b>I was almost certain that loneliness was a disease. An infectious, disgusting illness that was slow to creep into your system and overtake you, even though you tried to fight it off the best you could</b><br><br>After Ashlyn's twin, Gabby, died Ashlyn's mom made her go live with her father and his family. Her father was never there for her or Gabby. She didn't want to go. So on the bus ride, she gets up to go to the bathroom and she sees a beautiful blue eyed man.<br><br><b>His eyes were so blue and filled with interest. For a second, I thought they were a passageway to a different world.<br>Beautiful.<br>Breathtaking.<br>Brilliant.<br>Blue eyes.<br>I sighed.<br>Maybe they were a passageway to a better world</b><br><br>After they get off it was a brief conversation. But, Daniel invited her to go see his band, Romeo's Quest, perform. And my are they good. Ashlyn goes and has the most wonderful time. For a second she just got lost in the music, and his blue eyes. Her and Daniel just clicked. <br><br><b>“You know what I like about you so far?” <br><br>“What’s that?”<br><br>“Everything”</b><br><br>Since Ashlyn had health problems, she had to miss school. So she's a senior even though she's 19. So starting school in a town that she hates, with a vice principle of a father, with people she doesn't know, without her sister, and getting bullied for having boobs isn't so bad right? <br>Guess again, what tops it all off is that the blue eyed angle turned out to be a teacher, and she has him for AP English.<br><br>They try though, they try to push each other away. But they're in too deep to just push it aside.<br><br><b>“I don’t want to be your friend,” he said. We breathed in together and exhaled in harmony. “I want to be yours, I want you to be mine, and I hate that we can’t be us. Because I think we were meant to be us.”</b><br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpsapuhaman.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445779786i/16702242._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsapuhaman.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Their feelings just keep getting stronger and stronger. And the stronger it gets the harder it becomes. But it's impossible to stay away, because he's her golden and she's his light.<br><br><b>“He filled me back up, giving me life, giving me meaning, giving me him. I was shocked by his ability to awaken my spirit each and every time we were near one another. He was discovering all of my weaknesses and making them strong.”</b><br><br>By now I'm pretty sure that Brittainy Cherry is a kickass writer. And no doubt that she's now one of my favorite authors. Between this one and <i>The Air he Breathes</i> I'm pretty sold. <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6846430099597649859" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Amy | Foxy Blogs" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs"><img alt="Amy | Foxy Blogs" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1366176904p2/9955253.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/949429078?book_show_action=true">May 27, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy | Foxy Blogs" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy | Foxy Blogs" href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs">Amy | Foxy Blogs</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Amy | Foxy Blogs by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/5107700-jen">Jen</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=conquer-my-tbr-in-2015">conquer-my-tbr-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=forbidden">forbidden</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=2015-books">2015-books</a>,
