        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer949429078" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10956070188019146789">FOUR POINT FIVE STARS<br/><br/>FORBIDDEN ROMANCE!!! That is always a favorite of mine. <br/><br/><b>
  <u>”When in doubt with what to say, go to Shakespeare. He always had a good thing or two to express.”</u>
</b> <br/>Mr. Daniels is Ashlyn’s teacher but their attraction started long before either one knew what the other person was (student / teacher). They’re close in age with only being 3 years apart… so while it’s not a huge age gap they still have to contend with the whole student / teacher taboo. <b>”It wasn’t the age that was stop</b></span>
  <span id="freeText10956070188019146789" style="display:none">FOUR POINT FIVE STARS<br><br>FORBIDDEN ROMANCE!!! That is always a favorite of mine. <br><br><b>
  <u>”When in doubt with what to say, go to Shakespeare. He always had a good thing or two to express.”</u>
</b> <br>Mr. Daniels is Ashlyn’s teacher but their attraction started long before either one knew what the other person was (student / teacher). They’re close in age with only being 3 years apart… so while it’s not a huge age gap they still have to contend with the whole student / teacher taboo. <b>”It wasn’t the age that was stopping us - it was the occupation.”</b> <br><br><b>
  <u>”1) Who are you today? 2) Where do you see yourself in five years? 3) What do you want to be when you grow up?”</u>
</b><br>Mr. Daniels AP English class was posed with these questions. Who I am today is definitely not who I was 5 years ago. Five years ago I didn’t even know Goodreads existed. So, it makes me wonder in another five years what I’ll be doing. Sorry for the digression, I just found those questions intriguing because so much change happens in a five year period. <br><br><b>
  <u>”But the truth is, it’s not romantic - being someone’s secret.”</u>
</b><br>Mr. Daniels and Ashlyn weren’t the only ones having a secret relationship. I really enjoyed the complexities of the other supporting characters and finding out about their struggles. Not only was the student / teacher relationship forbidden but so was another relationship. Both of these forbidden relationships have a lot of pain that comes from never being able to show your love towards that person in public. Hiding behind closed doors loses it’s appeal as people’s feelings get hurt. However these two forbidden relationships showed how love knows no bounds.<br><br><b>
  <u>”It hurt to cry. It hurt to be alive.”</u>
</b><br>Both the heroine and the hero dealt with more tragedy than most people their age have had to deal with. Their story is one of healing and believing in one another. Having that person in your corner who will fight for you no matter what is invaluable. <br><br><b>Loving Mr. Daniels</b> is a great forbidden romance. It had one of my favorite things incorperated into it… letters. I love when letters, emails, text are part of a story. It gives another ‘secret’ look in the person’s life. <br><br><b>STANDALONE</b> <br><br><a href="http://foxyblogs.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408724793i/10887518.png" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> </span>

        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=cried-big-fat-ugly-tears">cried-big-fat-ugly-tears</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer920070049" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6668220177032099335">*****5 Beautiful. Breathtaking. Brilliant. Stars*****<br/>(BR with Melissa and Dee)<br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/d56f64005374b6e55095cc8bb00ae68e_zps2322ea39.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405839134i/10459788._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo d56f64005374b6e55095cc8bb00ae68e_zps2322ea39.jpg' width='370' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>This has got to be one of THE BEST books I have read in 2014.<br/>I'm going to put this in the <b>TOP THREE</b> category.<br/>If the writing is so beautiful that I find myself highlighting practically the entire book, then to me, the book is pure MAGIC!!<br/><b>"Loving Mr. Daniels"</b> is my <b>GOLDEN</b>!!!!<br/><br/><br/><br/>Ashlyn Jennings is a beautiful 19 year old girl, who has just lost her best friend in the entire world.<br/>Her twin sister, Gabby, just recently die</span>
  <span id="freeText6668220177032099335" style="display:none">*****5 Beautiful. Breathtaking. Brilliant. Stars*****<br>(BR with Melissa and Dee)<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/d56f64005374b6e55095cc8bb00ae68e_zps2322ea39.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405839134i/10459788._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo d56f64005374b6e55095cc8bb00ae68e_zps2322ea39.jpg" width="370" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>This has got to be one of THE BEST books I have read in 2014.<br>I'm going to put this in the <b>TOP THREE</b> category.<br>If the writing is so beautiful that I find myself highlighting practically the entire book, then to me, the book is pure MAGIC!!<br><b>"Loving Mr. Daniels"</b> is my <b>GOLDEN</b>!!!!<br><br><br><br>Ashlyn Jennings is a beautiful 19 year old girl, who has just lost her best friend in the entire world.<br>Her twin sister, Gabby, just recently died from her battle with cancer.<br>She's lost, devastated, and her world is about to be flipped upside down, when she learns her mother is sending her off to Wisconsin to live with her estranged father, who left them when she and Gabby were five. He's never come to visit or call them in all the time he's been gone from their lives.<br>Her relationship with her mom is strained and Ashlyn believes that her mom wishes it was she who had died instead of Gabby.<br><br><br><br>Gabby's boyfriend, Bentley, delivers to Ashley, a box filled with some of her prized possessions plus a bucket list with numbered letters for her.<br>Every time she crosses something off the list, she gets to read a letter from her sister.<br><br><br>On the train ride from Chicago to Wisconsin, Ashlyn sees a gorgeous man/boy or as she called him "Banmoy". His blue eyes captivate her.<br><br><b>Beautiful. Breathtaking. Brilliant. Blue eyes.</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/268bc78de08ae6f98ecb134bb55ea515_zpsfb1a5a98.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405839134i/10459789._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 268bc78de08ae6f98ecb134bb55ea515_zpsfb1a5a98.jpg" width="370" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Daniel Daniels strikes up a conversation with the beautiful girl with the sad green eyes when they arrive at their destination.<br>He invites her to come to the bar his band is playing at, the following weekend.<br>The chemistry between these two is undeniable.<br><br><br>Ashlyn is very much affected by her sister's death and having to move in with a father she has deep resentment for and abandonment issues with, I have to say I was really impressed at how strong she was.<br>Her dad has a new family and she, of course, feels that he just replaced her and Gabby with his step children.<br><br><br>There were numerous secondary characters that were developed so perfectly that I actually enjoyed their scenes and think that the author has plenty of material for follow up books if she wanted to make this a series.<br><br><br>I loved Ryan and Hailey.<br>The step brother and sister.<br>Ryan!! OMG. That boy tugged at my heart strings and never let go.<br>I cried many tears for him!!<br><br><br>Now back to my most favorite part of the story...Daniel!!<br>Daniel is gorgeous.<br>He's a musician!!<br>He's freaking brilliant and quotes Shakespeare!!<br>Ashlyn also is a Shakespeare fanatic.<br>So of course this is another reason why they just seem to be made for each other.<br>But there's one <b>BIG</b> problem.<br>Daniel is her AP English teacher!!<br>Oh I just love a good Student/Teacher love affair!!<br><br><br>There were parts of this story that reminded me of "Slammed", but only slightly.<br><br><br>There will be angst because of the whole, student/teacher relationships are forbidden deal, but Ashlyn and Daniel are so enamored of each other that it will be quite impossible for them to stay apart.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/1f698a312da3fc95644c9166df14ee37_zps1da08d4c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405839134i/10459790._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 1f698a312da3fc95644c9166df14ee37_zps1da08d4c.jpg" width="370" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I loved almost everything about this book.<br>The writing was exquisite!!<br>If I were to post all the quotes that I adored in my review, it would probably be a ten pager.<br>At this point, I know I have gone on too long but I can't even express just how affected I am by this story.<br>There are no amount of words that can truly express how I feel!<br>It is books like this, that have my heart soaring and makes me believe firmly that there is NOTHING better than coming across a fantastic story that leaves you utterly breathless.<br><br><br>I am also so very happy that I read this with my two loveys!!<br>What's better than reading a PHENOMENAL book with FABULOUS friends??!!!<br><br>If you haven't read this book, you need to bump it up your TBR!<br>Don't let any more time go by before you pick this one up!!<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6668220177032099335" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

  <span id="freeText8596793148748582832" style="display:none"><b>...5++++++ brilliant, brilliant stars from me...</b><br><br>Oh my God, what an emotional ride was that!!!<br>Especially in the last 50pages, i was crying like a baby... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385284070ra/7117393.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>If you could see me right now, you could see red, puffy eyes glistering from the tears... <br>But every single tear that slip down on my cheeks, was worthy...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428670686ra/14463515.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>That was a <u>GREAT</u> book and I'm pretty, pretty sure that this book just stole a part of my soul...<br>How i'm goin' to survive after that story??????<br><br>I want to tell you so much things about that marvellous book, but at the same time i don't want to tell you anything.... It was a heartbroken story, but a wonderfull one...<br><br>All the characters was complicating and their lives were so screwed up...But they were real, authentic persons... <br><br><b>"We were made perfectly imperfect."</b><br><br>Do you think that in real life is everything good and without pain or any kind of problems???? <br>No, my friends! Everyone's life is fucked up in one or another way... <br>Ashlyn reminds me myself in many things!!! I feel connented with this story...<br>I know that the pain in some points was unbareable, but that is the thing that make that book unforgetable...<br><br>In a world full of losses and broken hearts, Aslyn and Daniel found each other and the pain calmed down... <br>In a world that they thought that nothing existed anymore, they found in each other the strength to remain in life and keep fighting... They were each other's Golden...<br><br><b>“I want to be yours, I want you to be mine, and I hate that we can’t be us. Because I think we were meant to be us.”</b><br><br>I really don't want to reveal you many things for the plot, i just wanna tell you some of the things i liked in simply words...<br><i>I really loved Gabby's letters, they were so sentimental and funny...<br>I loved the way that the two of them connected and win the battle for their painfull souls...<br>I loved that in a crushed future, Aslyn find two allies beside her...<br>I hated what Ryan did to himself even though i loved him more than everyone in this book...<br>I liked the William Shakespeare's quotes...<br>I liked the double problem...<br>I liked... EVERY. SINGLE. WORD. in this book...</i><br>That story will stay with me... <b>forever, forever and always,always!</b> <br><br>You should read this story, guys!!! You may need a lot of tissues but you will love every single moment...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426192614ra/13986337.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Promise, Promise</b></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('NLx28swozt9LvHO15scMOkDBIHBWyKRsWV34YzsygjqCF8Yr+qu/UswaCFspAW5dRjsx8fHTSxA6Z8NjJX2TbA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('WkzBDvyh9mk56BUgir4HeyLgXsLn5ZD7UKyKOp0nXuDs53HXyiKH5L5Obs5FeGUcJBpPQ0D+f4czlrE6g2hPtg==')})
  }
